TO NAYAGIO THS KIXLHS To 3ulo auto pou drosize to metwpo mou
tis wres pou to meshmeri purwne tis fleves
se 3ena xeria 8elei an8isei. Par' to, sou to xarizw
des, einai 3ulo lemonias..."
Akousa th fwnh ka8ws ekoitaza sth 8alassa na 3exwrisw
ena karavi pou to voulia3an edw kai xronia
to'legan"Kixlh" ena mikro nauagio ta katartia,
spasmena, kumatizane lo3a sto va8os, san plokamia
h mnhmh oneirwn, deixnontas to skari tou
stoma 8ampo kapoiou megalou khtous nekrou
svhsmeno sto nero. Megalh aplwnountan galhnh.
Ki alles fwnes siga-siga me th seira tous
akolou8hsan yi8uroi ftenoi kai diyasmenoi
pou evgainan apo tou hliou t' allo meros, to skoteino
8a'leges gureuan na pioun aima mia stala
htane gnwrimes ma den mporousa na tis 3exwrisw.
Ki hr8e h fwnh tou gerou, auth thn eniwsa
peftontas sthn kardia ths meras
hsuxh, san akinhth:
"Ki a, me dikasete na piw farmaki, euxaristw to to dikio sas 8a'nai to dikio mou pou na phgainw gurizontas se 3enous topous, ena stroggulo li8ari. To 8anato ton protimw - poios paei gia to kalutero o 8eos to 3erei". Xwres tou hliou kai den mporeite n' antikrisete ton hlio.
Xwres tou an8rwpou kai den mporeite n' antikrisete ton an8rwpo TO FwS Ka8ws pernoun ta xronia
plh8ainoun oi krites pou se katadikazoun'
ka8ws pernoun ta xronia kai kouventiazeis me ligoteres fwnes,
vlepeis ton hlio m alla matia'
3ereis pws ekeinoi pou emeinan, se gelousan,
to paramilhma ths sarkas, o omorfos xoros
pou teleiwnei sth gumnia.
Opws, th nuxta strivontas sthn ermh dhmosia,
a3afna vlepeis na gualizoun ta matia enos zwou
pou efugan kiolas, etsi niw8eis ta matia sou'
ton hlio ton koitas, epeita xanesai mes sto skotadi'
o dwrikos xitwnas
pou aggi3ane ta daxtula sou kai lugise san ta vouna,
einai ena marmaro sto fws, ma to kefali tou einai sto skotadi.
Ki autous pou afhsan thn palaistra gia na paroun ta do3aria
kai xtuphsan to 8elhmatiko mara8wnodromo
ki ekeinos eide th sfendonh n' armenizei sto aima
n' adeiazei o kosmos opws to feggari
kai na marainountai ta nikhfora perivolia'
tous vlepeis mes ston hlio, pisw ap' ton hlio.
Kai ta paidia pou kanan makrovoutia ap' ta mpastounia
phgainoun san adraxtia gne8ontas akomh,
swmata gumna vouliazontas mesa sto mauro fws
m' ena nomisma sta dontia, kolumpwntas akomh,
ka8ws o hlios ravei me velonies malamatenies
pania kai 3ula ugra kai xrwmata pelagisia'
akomh twra katevainoune lo3a
pros ta xalikia tou vu8ou
oi aspres lhku8oi.
Aggeliko kai mauro, fws,
gelio twn kumatwn stis dhmosies tou pontou,
dakrusmeno gelio,
se vlepei o gerontas ikeths
phgainontas na draskelisei tis aorates plakes
ka8reftismeno sto aima tou
pou gennhse ton E teoklh kai ton Poluneikh.
Aggelikh kai maurh, mera'
h glufh geyh ths gunaikas pou farmakwnei to fulakismeno
vgainei ap' to kuma drosero klwnari stolismeno stales.
Tragoudhse mikrh Antigonh, tragoudhse, tragoudhse...
de sou milw gia perasmena, milw gia thn agaph'
stolise ta mallia sou me t' agka8ia tou hliou,
skoteinh kopela'
h kardia tou Skorpiou vasileye,
o turannos mesa ap' ton an8rwpo exei fugei,
ki oles oi kores tou pontou, Nhrhides, Graies
trexoun sta lampurismata ths anaduomenhs'
opoios pote tou den agaphse 8' agaphsei,
sto fws'
kai eisai s' ena megalo spiti me polla para8ura anoixta
trexontas apo kamara se kamara, den 3erontas apo pou na koita3eis prwta,
giati 8a fugoun ta peuka kai ta ka8reftismena vouna kai to titivisma twn pouliwn

8' adeiasoun ta matia sou ap' to fws ths meras
pws stamatoun 3afnika ki ola mazi ta tzitzikia.

ANAGNWSMA PRWTO
H PORE IA PROS TO ME TWPO
3hmerwnontas t' Agianniou, me thn aurio twn fwtwn, lavame
th diatagh na kinhsoume pali mprosta, gia ta merh opou den
exei ka8hmerines kai skoles. E prepe, leei, na piasoume tis
grammes pou kratousane ws tote oi Artinoi, apo Xeimarra
ws Tepeleni. Logw pou ekeinoi polemousane ap' thn prwth
mera, sunexeia, kai eixan meinei skedon oi misoi kai den
antexane allo.

Dwdeka meres kiolas eixame meis pio pisw, sta xwria.
Ki apanw pou sunh8ize t' auti mas pali sta gluka tri3imata
ths ghs, kai deila sullavizame to gavgisma tou skulou h ton
axo ths makrinhs kampanas, na pou htan anagkh, leei, na
gurisoume sto mono axoloi pou 3erame: sto argo kai sto varu
twn kanoniwn, sto 3ero kai sto grhgoro twn poluvolwn.

Nuxta panw sth nuxta vadizame astamathta, enas pisw
ap' ton allo, idia tufloi. Me kopo 3ekollwntas to podari apo
th lasph, opou, fores, ekatovouliaze isame to gonato. E peidh
to pio suxna yixalize stous dromous e3w, ka8ws mes sthn yuxh
mas. Kai tis liges fores opou kaname stash na 3ekourastoume,
mhte pou allazame kouventa, monaxoi sovaroi ki amilhtoi,
feggontas m' ena mikro dadi, mia-mia emoirazomastan th stafida.
H fores pali, an htan voleto, luname viastika ta rouxa kai
3unomastan me lussa wres polles, oso na tre3oun ta aimata.
Ti mas eixe anevei h yeira ws to laimo, ki htan auto pio ki ap' thn
kourash anupoferto. Telos, kapote, akougotane sta skoteina h
sfurixtra, shmadi oti kinousame, kai pali san ta za travousame
mprosta na kerdisoume dromo, prixou 3hmerwsei kai mas valoune
stoxo t' aeroplana. E peidh o 8eos den katexe apo stoxous h
tetoia, ki opws to 'xe sunh8io tou, sthn idia pantote wra 3hmerwne
to fws.

Totes, xwmenoi mes stis rematies, gername to kefali apo to
meros to varu, opou de vgainoune oneira. Kai ta poulia mas
8umwnan, pou de diname taxa shmasia sta logia tous - isws kai
pou askhmizame xwris aitia thn plash. Allhs loghs emeis xwriates,
m' allw logiw 3inaria kai siderika sta xeria mas, pou 3orkismena
na 'nai.

Dwdeka meres kiolas, eixame meis pio pisw sta xwria koita3ei
se ka8refth, wres polles, to guro tou proswpou mas. Ki apanw
pou sunh8ize 3ana to mati ta gnwrima palia shmadia, kai deila
sullavizame to xeilo to gumno h to xortato apo ton upno magoulo,
na pou th deuterh th nuxta sampws pali allazame, thn trith akomh
pio polu, thn usterh, thn tetarth, pia fanero, den eimastan oi idioi.
Mone sa na phgainame mpoulouki anakato, 8arrouses, ap' oles tis
genies kai tis xronies, alloi twn twrinwn kairwn ki alloi polla paliwn, 
pou 'xan leukanei ap' ta perissia genia. Kapetanaioi agelastoi me to
kefalopani, kai papades 8eria, loxies tou 97 h tou 12, mpaltatzhdes
vlosuroi panou ap' ton wmo seiwntas to peleki, apelates kai
skoutaroforoi me to aima epanw tous akomh Bourgarwn kai Tourkwn.
Oloi mazi, dixws milia, xronous ametrhtous agkomaxwntas plai-plai,
diavainame tis raxes, ta faraggia, dixws na logariazoume allo tipote.
Giati ka8ws otan varoun apanwtes anapodies tous idious tous
an8rwpous panta, sunh8an sto Kako, telos tou allazoun onoma, to
len Grammeno h Moira - etsi ki emeis eproxwrousame isia panou s'
auto pou legame Katara, opws 8a legame Antara h Sunnefo. Me
kopo 3ekollwntas to podari apo th lasph opou polles fores
ekatovouliaze isame to gonato. E peidh to pio suxna, yixalize stous
dromous e3w ka8ws mes sthn yuxh mas.

Ki oti hmastan sima polu sta merh opou den exei ka8hmerines
kai skoles, mhte arrwstous kai gerous, mhte ftwxous kai plousious,
to katalavainame. Giati ki o vrontos pera, kati san pisw ap' ta vouna,
dunamwne oloena, toso pou ka8ara sto telos na diavazoume to argo
kai to varu twn kanoniwn, to 3ero kai to grhgoro twn poluvolwn.
Ystera kai giati oloena pio suxna, tuxaine twra n' apantoume, ap' t'
allo meros va 'rxontai, oi arges oi sunodeies me tous lavwmenous.
Opou api8wnane xamou ta foreia oi nosokomoi, me ton kokkino stauro
sto perivraxiwnio, ftunontas mesa stis palames, kai to mati tous agrio
gia tsigaro. Ki opou san akougane gia pou travousame, kounousan to
kefali, arxinwntas istories gia shmeia kai terata. Omws emeis to mono
pou prosexame htan ekeines oi fwnes mesa sta skoteina, pou anevainan,
kautes akomh apo thn pissa tou vu8ou h to 8eiafi. "Oi, oi mana mou","
oi, oi mana mou", kai kapote, pio spania, ena pnixto mousounisma, idio
roxalhto, pou 'legan, osoi 3erane, einai autos o rogxos tou 8anatou.

Htan fores pou esernane mazi tous ki aixmalwtous, molis
piasmenous liges wres prin, sta 3afnika giourousia pou kanan ta peripola.
Brwmousane krasi ta xnwta tous, ki oi tsepes giomates konserva h sokolates.
Omws emeis den eixame, oti kommena ta giofuria pisw mas, kai ta liga moularia
mas ki ekeina anhmpora mesa sto xioni kai sth glistrada ths laspourias.

Telos kapoia fora, fanhkane makria oi kapnoi pou anevainan
meries-meries, ki oi prwtes ston orizonta kokkines, lamperes fwtovolides.

OI HMIONHGOI
Tis hmeres ekeines eftasan epitelous ustera apo treis swstes evdomades
oi prwtoi sta merh mas hmionhgoi. Kai elegan polla gia tis politeies pou
diavhkan, Delvino, Agioi Saranta, Korutsa. Kai 3efortwnan th regga kai

Oti den htan sunh8ismenoi kai tous etromaze to vrontisma sta vouna kai

Kai sunevhke totes enas ap' autous na 'xei mazi tou kati palies
efhmerides. Kai diavazame oloi aporhmenoi, m' olo pou to 'xame kiolas

vradu sta 8eatra legane tragoudia kai paristanane sth skhnh th zwh mas 
gia na xeirokrota o kosmakhs.

twra mesa stis erhmies agrieyei, kai, xwris na to leme, polu logariazame
ta xronia mas. Malista mia stigmh dakruse o loxias o Z whs ki ekane pera
ta xartia me tis eidhseis tou kosmou, anoigontas ta pente daxtula katapanw
tous. Kai oi alloi emeis de legame tipote, monaxa me ta matia tou deixname
kati san eugnwmosunh.
Tote o Leuterhs, pou tulige parekei tsigaro, karterika, sa na 'xe
parei apanw tou thn anhmporia olakerhs ths Oikoumenhs, gurise kai "Loxia"
eipe "ti varugkomas; Autoi pou 'nai tagmenoi gia th regga kai to xalva, s' auta
pantote 8a 3anagurizoun. Kai oi alloi sta defteria tous pou den exoune teleiwmo,
kai oi alloi sta krevatia tous ta malaka pou ta strwnoun ma den ta orizoun.
Alla katexe oti monaxa ekeinos pou paleuei to skotadi mesa tou 8a 'xei me8aurio
mertiko diko tou ston hlio". Kai o Z whs : "Ti loipon, 8arreis oti den exw ki egw
gunaika kai xwrafia kai vasana ths kardias pou ka8omai kai fulaw dwna stis
e3ories;" Tou apokri8hke o Leuterhs: "Auta pou den agapa kaneis, auta loxia
mou, na fovatai, ti ta 'xei apo ta prin xamena ki as ta sfiggei oso 8elei apanw
tou. Alla ta pramata ths kardias tropos den einai na xa8oun, ennoia sou, kai
gi ' auta oi e3ories douleuoun. Arga-grhgora keinoi pou einai nan ta vroun, 8a
ta vroun". Pali rwthse o loxias Z whs: "Kai poios les taxa tou logou sou oti 8an
ta vrei;" Tote o Leuterhs, arga, deixnontas me to daxtulo: "E su ki egw ki oti allo
dei3ei, aderfe mou, h wra touth pou mas akouei".
Kai eu8us akousthke ston aera h skoteinh sfurigmatia ths ovidas pou
eftane. Kai pesame oloi kataghs mproumuta, panw stis skarpes, oti gnwrizame
apo3w ta shmadia tou Aoratou, kai me t' auti mas orizame apo prin to meros opou
8a 'smige h fwtia to xwma n' anoi3ei kai na xu8ei. Kai den epeira3e h fwtia kanenan.
Kati moularia monaxa shkw8hkan sta pisina tous podaria kai alla taraxthkan

proswpa tous xlwma, kai 3efortwnan th regga kai to xalva koitazontas na

monon opla kai sidero kai fwtia
Monon opla kai sidero kai fwtia.

HR8AN
me ta xrusa seirhtia
ta peteina tou Borra kai ths Anatolhs ta 8hria !

kai sterna sto sukwti mou epanw erizontas
efugan.

kai gia mas ths fhmhs o kapnos,
amhn."

oloi akousame kai gnwrisame.
thn hxw akousame gnwrisame 3ana
me stegnh fwnh tragoudhsame :
Gia mas, to matwmeno sidero
kai tripla ergasmenh prodosia.
Gia mas h augh sto xalkwma
kai ta dontia ta sfigmena ws thn wra thn usterh
o dolos kai t' aorato gaggamo27.
Gia mas to sursimo ths ghs

twn matiwn h aponia

Adelfoi mas egelasan !
"Gi' autous, eipan, o kapnos ths 8usias,
kai gia mas ths fhmhs o kapnos,
amhn."
Alla su mes sto xeri mas to luxno tou astrou

8ura ths Paradeisos !
Thn isxu tou kapnou sto mellon vlepoume

ANAGNWSMA TRITO
H ME GALH E 3ODOS
Tis hmeres ekeines ekanan suna3h mustikh ta paidia kai lavane thn apofash,
epeidh ta kaka mantata plh8ainan sthn prwteuousa, na vgoun e3w se plateies me
to mono pragma pou tous eixe apomeinei : mia palamh topo katw apo t' anoixto
poukamiso, me tis maures trixes kai to stauroudaki tou hliou. Opou eixe kratos
h Anoi3h.
Kai epeidh simwne h mera pou to Genos eixe sunh8io na giortazei ton allo
Shkwmo, th mera pali ekeinh orisane gia thn E 3odo. Kai nwris evghkane
katamprosta ston hlio, me panou ws katou aplwmenh thn afovia sa shmaia, oi
neoi me ta prhsmena podia pou tous elegan alhtes. Kai akolou8ousane antres
polloi, kai gunaikes, kai lavwmenoi me ton epidesmo kai ta dekanikia. Opou evlepes
a3afna sthn oyh tous toses xarakies, pou 'leges eixane perasei meres polles mesa
se lighn wra.
Tetoias loghs apokoties, wstoso, ma8ainontes oi Alloi, sfodra taraxthkan.
Kai treis fores me to mati anametrwntas to exei tous, lavane thn apofash na vgoun
e3w se dromous kai se plateies, me to mono pragma pou tous eixe apomeinei: mia
phxh fwtia katw ap' ta sidera, me tis maures kanes kai ta dontia tou hliou. Opou
mhte klwnos mhte an8os, dakruo pote den evgalan. Kai xtupousane opou na 'nai,
sfalwntas ta vlefara me apognwsh. Kai h Anoi3h oloena tous kurieue. San na mhn
htane allos dromos panw s' olakerh th gh, gia na perasei h Anoi3h para monaxa
autos, kai na ton eixan parei amilhtoi, koitazontas polu makria, per' ap' thn akrh
ths apelpisias, th Galhnh pou emellan na ginoun, oi neoi me ta prhsmena podia pou
tous elegan alhtes, kai oi antres, kai oi gunaikes, kai oi lavwmenoi me ton epidesmo
kai ta dekanikia.
Kai perasane meres polles mesa se lighn wra. Kai 8erisane plh8os ta 8hria,
kai allous emazw3an. Kai thn allh mera esthsane ston toixo trianta.

I'

Pou otan oloi emeis pen8oume,
autos hlioforei.
Kai otan eirhnh aggeloume,
maxairoforei.
Kataproswpo mou oi neoi Ale3andreis exleuasan !

TO OIKOPE DO ME TIS TSOYKNIDE S
MIAN APO TIS ANHLIAGE S meres ekeinou tou xeimwna, ena prwi
Savvatou, swros autokinhta kai motosukletes ezwsane to mikro
sunoikismo tou Leuterh, me ta trupia tenekedenia para8ura kai
t' aulakia twn oxetwn ston dromo. Kai fwnes agries vganontas,
ekatevhkane an8rwpoi me xumenh thn oyh sto moluvi kai mallia
oloisa idio axero. Prostazontas na sunaxtoun oi antres oloi sto
oikopedo me tis tsouknides. Kai htan armatwmenoi apo panou ws
katou, me tis mpoukes xamhla strammenes kata to mpoulouki. Kai
megalos fovos epiane ta paidia, epeidh tuxaine, sxedon ola, na
katexoune kapoio mustiko sthn tseph h sthn yuxh tous. Alla
tropos allos den htane, kai xreos thn anagkh kanontas, lavane 8esh
sth grammh, kai oi an8rwpoi me to moluvi sthn oyh, to axero sta
mallia kai ta konta maura podhmata, 3etuli3ane gurw tous to
surmatoplegma. Kai koyane sta duo ta sugnefa, oso pou to
xiononero arxise na peftei, kai ta sagonia me kopo kratousane
ta dontia sth 8esh tous, mhpws tous fugoun h spasoune.
Tote, ap t' allo meros fanhke arga vadizontas na 'rxetai
Autos me to Svhsmeno Proswpo, pou shkwne to daxtulo ki oi wres
anatrixiazan sto megalo roloi twn aggelwn. Kai se opoion laxaine
na sta8ei mprosta, eu8us oi alloi ton arpazane kai ton esournane
xamou patwntas ton. Wspou eftase kapote h stigmh na sta8ei kai
mprosta ston Leuterh. Alla ekeinos de saleye. Shkwse mono arga
ta matia tou kai ta phge me mias toso makria - makria mesa sto
mellon tou - pou o allos eniwse to skounthma ki egeire pisw me
kintuno na pesei. Kai skuliazontas, ekane n' anashkwsei to mauro
tou pani, nan tou ftusei katamoutra. Ma pali o Leuterhs de saleye.
Panw se keinh th stigmh, o Megalos 3enos, autos pou akolou8ouse
me ta tria seirhtia sto giaka, sthrizontas ta xeria sth mesh tou,
kagxase: oriste, eipe, oriste oi an8rwpoi pou 8eloune , leei, n'
alla3oune thn poreia tou kosmou ! Kai mh gnwrizontas oti elege thn
alh8eia o dustuxhs, kataproswpo treis fores tou katafere to
mastigio. Alla trith fora o Leuterhs de saleye. Tote, tuflos apo th
ligh perash pou 'xe h dunamh sta xeria tou, o allos, mh gnwrizontas
ti prattei, travh3e to peristrofo kai tou to vronthse surriza
sto de3i tou auti.
Kai polu troma3ane ta paidia, kai oi an8rwpoi me to moluvi sthn
oyh kai ta konta maura podhmata, kerwsan. E peidh phgane k' hr8ane
gurw ta xamospita, kai se polles meries to pissoxarto epese kai
fanhkane makria, pisw apo ton hlio, oi gunaikes na klaine gonatistes,
panw s' ena ermo oikopedo, gemato tsouknides kai maura phxta aimata.
E nw shmaine dwdeka akrivws to megalo roloi twn aggelwn.

koprokratoun to mellon.

mnhmoneuete Dionusio Solwmo
kai mnhmoneuete Ale3andro Papadiamanth.
H lalia pou den 3erei apo yema
8' anapausei to proswpo to marturiou

ANAGNWSMA PE MPTO
H AYLH TWN PROBATWN
E ipen o laos mou: to dikaio pou mou dida3an epra3a kai idou aiwnes
apokama n' apantexw e3w apo thn kleisth 8ura ths aulhs twn provatwn.
Gnwrize th fwnh mou to poimnio kai sthn ka8e sfurigmatia mou
anaphdouse kai velaze. Alloi omws, kai polles fores io idioi pou peneuane
thn karteria mou, apo dentra kai mantres phdwntas, epatousane prwtoi
to podi autoi mes sth mesh ths aulhs twn provatwn. Kai idou panta gumnos
egw kai xwris poimnio kanena, stenazen o laos mou. Kai sta dontia tou
gualizen h arxaia peina, kai h yuxh tou etri3e panw sthn pikra ths ka8ws
pou trizei epanw sto xaliki to arvulo tou apelpismenou.
Totes autoi pou katexoune ta polla, n' akousoune tetoio tri3imo,
troma3an. E peidh to ka8e shmadi kataleptws gnwrizoune kai suxna, milia
makria diavazoune sto sumferon tous. Pareu8us loipon ta pedila t'
apathla pode8hkan. Kai misoi pianontas tous allous misous, apo to 'na
kai t' allo meros travousane, tetoia logia legontas: a3ia kai kala ta erga
sas, kai oriste auth auth pou vlepete h 8ura h kleisth ths aulhs twn
provatwn. Ashkwste to xeri kai mazi sas emeis, kai frontida dikh mas h
fwtia kai to sidero. Spitika mh fovaste, famelies mh lupaste, kai pote
se giou h patera h mikrou aderfou th fwnh, pisw mh kanete. E ide tuxei
kaneis apo sas ki h fovh8ei ki h luph8ei ki h kanei pisw, na 3erei: epanw
tou h fwtia pou ferame kai to sidero.
Kai to logo tous prin aposwsoun eixe parei n' allazei o kairos,
makria sto mauradi twn nefwn kai sima sto kopadi twn an8rwpwn. Sa na
perase ageras xamhla voggwntas kai n' apori3e adeia ta kormia, dixws
mia stala 8umhsh. To kefali mplavo kai alala ayhla strammeno, ma to
xeri va8ia mesa sthn tseph, grapwmeno apo kommati sidero, ths fwtias
h ap' t' alla, po 'xoun th muth souglerh kai thn koyh a8era. Kai vadizane
katapanou ston enan o allos, mh gnwrizontas o enas ton allo. Kai
shmadeue kata patera o gios kai kat' aderfou mikrou o megalos. Pou
polla spitika pomeinane sth mesh, kai polles gunaikes apanwta duo kai
treis fores mauroforesane. Kai pou an ekanes na vgeis ligaki parao3w,
tipote. Mono ageras vouizontas mesa sta mesodokia kai sta liga kamena
li8aria meries-meries oi kapnoi voskwntas ta koufaria twn skotwmenwn.
Mhnes trianta treis kai pleon vasth3e to Kako. Pou th 8ura
xtupousane n' anoi3oune ths aulhs twn provatwn. Kai fwnh provatou
den akousthke parextos epanw sto maxairi. Kai fwnh 8uras oute,
parextos sthn wra pou 'gerne mes stis floges tis usteres na kaei.
E peidh autos o laos mou h 8ura kai autos o laos mou h aulh kai to
poimnio twn provatwn.

8amna kai koufoli8ia.

kai tou perivolarh

vouliazoun oi troxoi.

ola t' alh8ina
ta futra, xortasmena!

Aima 8a tre3h... Eisai a3ios, sa 8elhshs.

Tou elegxou kai ths steiras hdonhs

Kai s' eme (pou oso duo xeimwnies, toso, alh8eia,

Ax, dakrua oso naurw, mou xanetai h yuxh|

ap' to lila kai s' allo pio lila, kai pali

Katw ap' tis elies, oi wres siwphles
pairnoune th mera pe8amenh.
Katw ap' tis lignes, tis skorpies agrielies,
afwno, pikro to leiyano diavainei.

Ax, th neioth sou, 3an8oula mou Erwmenh,
me thn wxra tou exei o 8anatos vammenh.

Mes sto agerino, pou feugei, deilino,
to portraito ths ston hlio pws xlwmainei!
Sure! Sth zwhn akomh n' agrupnw
- etsi moumellen, agaph staurwmenh!

3evgalan th Mera pe8amenh.
Mas exwrisan, xlwmoula mou erwmenh!

K' ein' h nuxta pia, pou marturikia, 
gnwrimh, xwris musthrio, vasileuei...
K' ein' h nuxta pia, pou krua kai plhxtikia,
sta va8eia, va8eia mou dunasteuei.

Akou: sigana paramilei ena fullo!
Kapoio fws mavu glustra ap' ta monopatia.
w yuxh mou, w sfalise ta matia!

Polukatoikhmeno einai to rafi
me tis glastres, phxta ta fulla, kai ta klwnia|
glastres ki' ws mes sthn petrinh, xamw, th skafh,
ki' o fukos, geitonas, skounta ta pelargonia.

To mousklo, velonia th velonia, kai vriskei
pantou thn koufia riza na kataskepazh.
Des, k' h fragkosukia pou tremoun ths oi diskoi,
3wtikh sarka agka8erh, prasinh, moiazei.

K' e3afna, kapou edw sta xorta, h san pio pera,
fushma oligo kinhse na ta peira3h:
esugxuse alafra ton a8umon aera.
Xalaei ta fulla, viazetai, xalaei thn ta3h,

k' h staxterh, h perpathmenh h prasinada,
to melagxoliko koritsi pou diavazei,
ta hmerina ta marmara, h periplokada,
to spitiko perivolaki, sunnefiazei.

Muristika, potistika gurw ap' th vrush,
parataira, esugklinan- k' e3anaka8hsan|
kati 3eno sa nar8e na sugkatoikhsh|
kai mia fouxta spourgitia omognwma eskorpisan...

Ma eleiye ki' olas. Ma htane mia apath akoma,
mouxrwma-k' eluwse, k' iskios aplhs hmeras.
Gia th sarka pikros, ax! pikros ki' ws to stoma,
tou prwtoxinopwrou perasen o ageras...

Me xwris fwtoxusies, m' oligous hxous
vrexei, "epi dikaious kai adikous"...
vrexei sthn plateia, sth fulakh,
- oikoumenikh vroxh, euaggelikh.

Brexei sta vagonia (w eu8umia)
pou gurnane ap' ta Nosokomeia|
kai stis profhteies tou Kazamia
("troph tou kairou pros noton... trikumia...").

Brexei sta nera, vrexei sta futra,
vrexei stis gazies sou, ma8htra!
Brexei- tupika, kai dixws shmasia...
Brexei stis ma8htres sou, gazia!

Stou kenou ton kuklo katevainei
ths vroxhs sou h sunefaptomenh...
St' ouranou th mataihn agkalia
trigwna, ta e3orista poulia.

Xinopwrines Ishmeries
(w oi vroxes, w oi trigwnometries!).
Kai na mh mporw (me sugxwreis)
na sou ma8w ekeina pou aporeis.

Brexei, Kuriakh... Kaneis, kaneis,
allo apo "gnwstous" kai "suggeneis"...
Krimas th xara, krimas th sxolh!
Den exei sergiani sto pervoli,

pou 8a pagainorxetai, skuftos,
sto staxti to mousama tou A u t o s !

Oi stixoi autoi mporei kai na 'nai oi teleutaioi
Oi teleutaioi stous teleutaious pou 8a graftoun
Giati oi melloumenoi poihtes de zoune pia
Autoi pou 8a milousane pe8anan oloi neoi
Ta 8livera tragoudia tous genhkane poulia
Se kapoion allon ourano pou lampei 3enos hlios
Genhkan agrioi potamoi kai trexoune sth 8alassa
Kai ta nera tous den mporeis na 3exwriseis
Sta 8livera tragoudia tous futrwse enas lwtos
Na gennh8oume sto xumo tou emeis pio neoi.

O lampros an8rwpos, o oikogeneiarxhs, o patriwths.

                                    antiproedrwn,

                                    proseferes.

Ena ka8e vdomada, 
sthn orismenh mera, 
panta sthn idian wra, 
tria vaporia wraia, 
h "Kleopatra", h "Semiramis" k' h "8eodwra", 
anoigountai ap' thn prokumaia 
stis ennea, 
panta gia ton Peraia, 
to Mprintizi kai to Triesti, 
panta. 

Xwris manouvres k' eligmous 
kai distagmous 
ki' anwfela sfurigmata, 
strefoune st' anoixta thn prwra, 
h "Kleopatra", h "Semiramis" k' h "8eodwra", 
san kapoioi kaloana8remmenoi 
pou feugoun apo ena saloni 
xwris anousies xeirayies 
kai perittes. 

Anoigountai ap' thn prokumaia 
stis ennea, 
panta gia ton Peraia, 
to Mprintizi kai to Triesti, 
panta -kai me to kruo kai me th zesth. 

Pane 
na mountzourwsoun ta galazia 
tou Aigaiou kai ths Mesogeiou 
me tous kapnous twn. 
Pane gia na skorpisoune topazia 
ta fwta tous mes' sta nera 
th nuxta. 
Pane 
panta m' an8rwpous kai mpagkazia... 

H "Kleopatra", h "Semiramis" k' h "8eodwra", 
xronia twra, 
kanoun ton idio dromo, 
ftanoun thn idia mera, 
feugoun sthn idian wra. 

Moiazoun upallhloi grafeiwn 
pou ginane xronometra, 
pou h porta ths douleias, 
an den tous dei mia mera na perasoun 
apo katw ths, 
mporei na pesei. 

(Otan o dromos einai panta idios 
ti taxa an einai se mia oloklhrh Mesogeio 
h ap' to spiti s' allh sunoikia;) 
H "Kleopatra", h "Semiramis" k' h "8eodwra" 
einai kairos kai xronia pane twra 
tou varemou pou enoiwsan thn turannia, 
na perpatoun panta ston idio dromo, 
na denoune panta sta idia limania. 

An hmoun egw ploiarxos, 
nai -si j'etais roi!- 
an hmoun egw ploiarxos 
sthn "Kleopatra", th "Semiramh", th "8eodwra", 
an hmoun egw ploiarxos 
me tessera xrusa galonia 
ki an m' afhnan sthn idia auth grammh 
tosa xronia, 
mia nuxta selhnofeggh, 
sth mesh tou pelagou, 
8' anevaina sto tetarto katastrwma 
ki enw 8' akougountan h mousikh 
pou 8a' paize sths prwths 8eshs ta salonia, 
me th megalh mou stolh, 
me ta xrusa mou ta galonia 
kai ta xrusa mou ta parashma, 
8a' grafa mian armonikotath kampulh 
apo to tetarto katastrwma 
mes' sta nera, 
etsi me ta xrusa mou, 
san asthr diattwn 
san hrws ane3hghtwn 8anatwn. 

1

Egw pou agapw tis nuxtes ws thn augh
vre8hka sto 3ediplwma mias allhs nuxtas
ki exw pia thn eikona ths na thn koitazw,
ta poulia mono leipoun, fantasmata,
ma ta 8umamai san troma3an
ki hr8an sth gefura gurw mou,

3anavlepontas to mproutzino xrwma pou ta petrwse
kai thn asprh san evaye etsi foresia mou.

sta ka8hmerina mou to fainomeno
otan esu thn idia stigmh
sto Sounio pou 'grafes
to fws ekeino sto skotadi,
stis eikones tous
se anamnhsh.
Eitan auta stis 19/6/35
anamesa 5 kai 6.40' to prwi.-

Otan vlepw kapoion na perpath epanw-katw, opws o makariths o Ber8eros, kai na meleta mian erwtikhn ekdikhsin, legw apo mesa mou: "Idou enas an8rwpos, pou etoimazetai na kamh mian anohsian!".
    Ka8enas thn kamnei me ton tropon tou. Allos foneuei. Alla o 8anatos einai musthrion. Allos autoktonei. Alla h autoktonia einai mia hli8ioths. Allos speudei na upandreu8h me to prwton adespoton 8hlu, pou sunanta eis ton dromon tou, fantazomenos oti ekdikeitai me ton tropon auton ekeinhn, pou epause na ton agapa. Auto einai 3ekardistikh kwmwdia. Allos grafei ena drama, eis to opoion kauthriazei tas gunaikas me pepuraktwmenon sidhron. Autos, aploustata ma3ilarwnetai. Yphr3en enas an8rwpos, o opoios, dia na ekdikh8h thn gunaika tou, kathrghsen, en stigmh paraforas, to fulon tou me thn maxairan tou dhmiou. Me auton geloun oi aiwnes. Kaneis, me mian le3in, den esta8h ikanos na ekdikh8h epa3iws mian gunaika eis ton kosmon auton.
    To pragma einai eue3hghton. Oloi oi ekdikhtai ths gunaikeias apistias energoun m' ena tropon esfalmenon eis thn vasin tou. Energoun dhladh m' ena tropon upervolika sovaron kai polu suxna tragikon. Protimoun thn tragwdian ekei, opou kat' e3oxhn 8a hto endedeigmenh h farsa. Ypoduontai ton ko8ornon tou tragwdou, enw o akatallhloteros an8rwpos dia na pai3h ena sovaron rolon eis to 8eatron ths zwhs einai o atuxhsas erasths. Kai, enw oregetai tas dafnas enos Talma, dexetai ta ma3ilaria ths plateias epi ths kefalhs tou. 
    Di' auto akrivws oi sofwteroi den peripatoun pia epanw-katw, meta thn prodosian h thn egkataleiyin, opws o makariths Ber8eros, kai den meletoun mian ekdikhsin. Shkwnontai apo to geuma, opou emisoteleiwsan to fagi twn, skoupizoun to stoma twn me thn petsetan, plhrwnoun kai feugoun, ws na mh tous sunevh tipote, afinontes enan allon n' apoteleiwsh thn merida twn. Etsi diaswzoun thn a3ioprepeian twn, xwris na meinoun kai entelws anekdikhtoi. Dioti gnwrizoun oti einai entelws peritton na ekdikhtai ka8enas xwrista thn aiwnian gunaika. Di' authn uparxoun oi ek 8eou apestalmenoi ekdikhtai, pou einai oi Don Zouan olwn twn topwn kai olwn twn epoxwn, kai oi opoioi den kamnoun allo, para na ekdikountai diarkws dia ton eauton tous kai dia tous allous. 
    En toutois, ofeilomen na kamwmen timhtikhn e3airesin dia ton an8rwpon, o opoios pro oligwn hmerwn epragmatopoihse prwtotupon ekdikhsin eis thn Akropolin authn ths koinotopias, pou einai ai A8hnai. Eidate apo tas efhmeridas, ti ekamen o megalofuhs autos. Ephge nukta eis thn 8uran ths apistou kai ths etoixokollhse mian epigrafhn: "Edw uparxei eulogia". Tipote allo! To allo prwi oi diavatai epernousan, estamatousan, ediavazan kai efeugan entromoi makrua. O galatas den ektuphse thn 8uran ekeino to prwi. O manavhs den estamathsen. O grammatokomisths, pou eferne mian erwtikhn epistolhn, thn e3anavalen eis ton sakkon tou kai efugen. O neos erasths, molis eplhsiasen eis thn gwnian tou dromou kai prin parelash akomh upo to 8rulikon para8uron, anekrouse me tropon prumnan kai den efanh pleon. Otan h apistos antelhf8h thn sumforan kai esteile na 3esxisoun thn katax8onian epigrafhn, hto pleon arga. O prodo8eis erasths eixen ekdikh8h! Kai eixen ekdikh8h kuriws, dioti h apistos ton efantazeto 3ekardismenon apo ta gelia eis mian gwnian tou dromou, en w 8a h8ele na ton fantas8h aphgxonismenon apo thn orofhn tou dwmatiou tou.
    Otan ton erwthsan eis thn Astunomian, diati proevh eis thn a8lian authn pra3in, legoun oti apekri8h afelestata:

    Kai h Astunomia apeluse ton erasthn kai esteile ton astuiatron na emvoliash thn erwmenhn, dia ka8e endexomenon kai dia thn hsuxian ths sunoikias. H farsa kai h ekdikhsis elave toioutotropws thn wraian ths sunexeian.

O Straths to stoixeio -etsi akougotane twra s' olo to nhsi, xronia kai xronia- den agapouse ton kosmo kai zouse pant' alarga ap' tous an8rwpous. Apo paidi moutsos sta Skopelitika karavia kai pio ustera nauths kai lostromos kai kapetanios, kai twr' akoma, pouxe parathsei tis 8alasses, geros ogdontarhs, ki epiase tous gialous, me th mikrh tou yarovarka, th "Maxw" -ths monaxokorhs tou t' onoma- den allaze ola ta kala tou kosmou me th mona3ia tou. Etsi tou kollhse kai to paranomi. O Straths to Stoixeio me t' onoma. wstos' o Straths den htane kai toso monaxos, sth mona3ia tou. Eixe tous suntrofous tou.     O Straths sth mona3ia tou eixe tous kaluterous suntrofous tou kosmou. Kai pws alliws; An8rwpos de sta8hke, pou na mporei na zhsei monaxos tou. Oute ta stoixeia, t' alh8ina stoixeia. HPAKLEITOS 

Me thn patrida tous demenh sta pania kai ta koupia ston anemo kremasmena 
Oi nauagoi koimh8hkan hmeroi san agrimia nekra mesa stwn sfouggariwn ta sentonia 
Alla ta matia twn fukiwn einai stramena sth 8alassa 
Mhpws tous 3anaferei o notias me ta freskovamena latinia 
Ki enas xamenos elefantas a3izei pantote pio polu apo duo sth8ia koritsiou pou saleuoun 
Mono n' anayoune sta vouna oi steges twn erhmokklhsiwn me to meraki tou aposperith 
Na kumatisoune ta poulia sths lemonias ta katartia 
Me ths kainourgias perpathsias to sta8ero aspro fushma 
Kai tote 8a 'r8oun aerhdes swmata kuknwn pou meinane aspiloi truferoi kai akinhtoi 
Mes stous odostrwthres twn magaziwn mesa stwn laxanokhpwn tous kuklwnes

Afou mataiws eperimena treis mhnes na me proskalesh kamia aeroporikh etaireia sto e3wteriko, anagkasthka na thlefwnhsw s' enan gnwsto mou nautiko praktora, mhpws uparxei elpida na paw sto eswteriko, estw katastrwma, alla upo ton oron na exh kai fai.
     O filos mou -Petros elegeto-, an8rwpos drasthrios, ta katafere, ki ena meshmeri pou gurisa spiti me maurh kardia apo ta lavara tou antikarkinikou agwnos, mou efere thn xarmosunon aggelia.
     - En ta3ei, mou eipe. Savvato apogeuma mexri Deutera prwi 8a kanhs krouaziera trellh. Suros, Thnos, Mukonos. Exeis 3anapaei;
     - Oxi.
     - Oriste 8aumasia eukairia na pas. Eisai euxaristhmenos;
     Den apanthsa amesws. Shmera h tetamenh katastasis epivallei sunesin kai oxi en8ousiasmous.
     - Den mporw na sou pw twra amesws, Petro mou. Prepei na to skef8w kai na sta8misw ta pragmata. Kanei na sou apanthsw aurio;
     - Pws den kanei, eipe o Petros. Ki efuge.
     Htan 8limmenh Paraskeuh otan mou to proteine. Perimena mexri 12 meshmeri tou Savvatou mhpws exoume newtera apo kamia allh etaireia, perasa viastikos duo-treis fores e3w ap' thn AIR FRANCE, anevhka LOYFT XANSA xwris apotelesma, eftasa mexri AI8IOPIAN AIPLA iN kai TOYPK XABA GIOLAPH ki ekana pws koitaw tis vitrines kai stis 12 1/2, otan eida ki apoeida pws 8a katsw Savvatokuriako sthn A8hna, phra ton Petro sto thlefwno:
     - Akouse Petro, etaktopoihsa tas ergasias mou. Twra eimai eleu8eros kai mallon 8a el8w. Ti wra feugei to ploion, eipes;
     - Stis 2 akrivws. 1 1/2 na eisai sto roloi. 8a se perimenw.
     Sto roloi hmoun 1 para tetarto, ntumenos polu spor. Ephra kai oligous spor, ptuwn tas floud, kai xazeuwn ta vapor. wraia vevaiws einai ta aeroplana, skef8hka, alla ti ta 8elete... Mono me to vapori ais8anesai asfaleia. Kai na voulia3h, pou leei o logos, me ligo kolumpi glutwneis. Pianesai apo kapou, vgaineis se kamia akth. Kamia fora swzontai monon duo, esu ki auth -wraiotath 3an8h me uperoxo swma-, kai glutwnete s' ena erhmo nhsi me xourmadies, kokkofoinikes, plousia vlasthsh ki e3wtika poulia, ki enw to uperoxo feggari 8' anevainh ston ourano, auth 8a sou tragoudah nostalgika tragoudia ths patridos ths kai 8a se nanourizh xa ideuontas sou ta mallia. O monos fovos s' autes tis periptwseis einai mhn emfanis8oun tipotis agrioi kannivaloi me dhlhthriwdh velh. M' auto 8elw na pw pws kai ta 8alassia ta3idia den einai ki auta asfalh 100%, alla nomizw pws kata kapoio tropo einai asfalestera apo to aeroplano. Epeita, mhpws ola ta nhsia exoun kannivalous; Mporei na sou tuxh kai nhsi teleiws akatoikhto. Auta einai zhthmata ka8arws tuxhs. Alla kai na emfanis8oun, 3erw na uperaspisw ton eauto mou kai ekeinhn. 8a polemhsw agria kai apofasistika ws Ellhn maxhths, skorpizwn ton 8anaton stous i8ageneis. 3eurw pws o agwn 8a einai anisos kai isws sullhf8w kai aixmalwtos kai 8a kaih o hlios otan 8a me metaferoun oi agrioi me alalagmous sthn kaluva tou arxhgou. 3erw apo twra malista ti 8a me rwthsh:
     - Pote hr8es edw;
     - Den 8a dwsw logariasmo se kanenan, 8a apanthsw.

     - Etsi 8elw...

     Oi mauroi e3hfanis8hsan ws dia mageias. O leukos Petros eurisketo mprosta mou.
     - Den exw tipota. Pame. Arghses, mwre Petro...
     Mpros o Petros pisw egw o mauros, mphkame ston "Kara iskakh".
     - Ela, mou eipe, na paroume kati sto mpar na sunel8hs. Ti 8a parhs;
     - Ti exei;
     - Ap' ola uparxoun ston "Kara iskakh".
     - E , tote as paroume ena Karaou iskakh, alla xwris soda.
     Katevaza se mikres goulies ton endo3o oplarxhgo, koitazontas gurw mou.
     - Poios einai autos, Petro; rwthsa, deixnontas mia fwtografia megalh.
     - O idiokthths tou ploiou Nomikos.
     - Xairomai pou kerdizoun oi dikhgoroi. Alles epoxes, tetoia ploia anhkon eis tous efoplistas. Eilikrina xairomai.
     - Ma einai o Nomikos ths etaireias...
     - Katalava. Gia vlaka m' exeis; Malista. O Nomikos sumvoulos ths etaireias. Ki ap' o,ti vlepw 8a plhrwnetai kala. Alliwtika de 8' agoraze toso megalo karavi. Den 8a mou fanh, loipon, ka8olou para3eno an aurio mou poun oti to tade ploio anhkei se zwgrafo. Bre Petro, den rwtas me tropo sthn etaireia auth an xreiazontai kallitexnes;
     - 8a rwthsw, eipe o Petros kai plhrwse ta pota. Ela na se paw twra sthn kampina sou...

     Mas sunesthse na doume duo-treis ekklhsies ka8ws kai thn ekklhsia ths Panagias tou Kampanh, gia na doume to idiorru8mo templo ths.
     Apo to arxontiko tou Kampanh vre8hkame sthn Nea Orleanh. Sthn plateia ths Mantws Maurogenous vrisketai to kentro "PAPALOS". Osoi exoun paei to 3eroun. Egw ta grafw gi' autous pou den phgan. O idiokthths tou einai enas Amerikanos zwgrafos kai pragmatikos filellhn, pou a3iopoihse ta panta.      Auta ola uparxoun sth megalh ai8ousa. Panw apo to mpar vrisketai enas megalos ka8refths, kamwmenos palios venetsianikos kai sunarmologhmenos se tetragwna kommatia. Aristera kai de3ia duo lampes, pou poios 3erei pws katwr8wse na tis vrh. Mhte se spitia pia uparxoun tetoies, mhte kai s' olo to Monasthraki na ya3ete den prokeitai na vrhte paromoies. Ki omws, o kataplhktikos autos xristianos vrhke 8 tetoies kai tis kotsarise pantou. Eftia3e kai duo megalous pagkous polu8rones, ru8mou ollando-mukoniatikou, eftia3e xamhla trapezia epimhkh ki aplwse xamw kokkines kai mple flokates, stolise me nautika 8emata ton toixo kai patinarise diakritika thn atmosfaira. Me duo logia, eftia3e me to tipota ena stolidi sto nhsi.
     Kurie Amerikane sunadelfe, pou agaphses toso polu th Mukono, sou vgazw to kapello kai proskunw. Eime8a oloi entos tou mellontos mas. Otan tragoudame empros stous ekfrastikous pinakes twn zwgrafwn otan skuvoume empros sta axura mias kammenhs polews otan prosetairizome8a thn yixala tou rigous eime8a oloi entos tou mellontos mas giati o,ti kai an epidiw3oume den einai dunaton na poume oxi na poume nai xwris to mellon tou proorismou mas opws mia gunaika den mporei na kamh tipote xwris thn purkagia pou kleinei mesa sth staxth twn podiwn ths. Osoi thn eidan den sta8hkan na enatenisoun oute ta sustrefomena khparia oute thn euwxia twn malliwn pou latreuthkan oute ta souraulia twn ergasthriakwn metaggisewn apo mia xwra se fleves kolpou 8ermou prostateuomenou apo ta egkosmia kai ta meltemia ths kuanhs antaugeias ligurwn par8enwn. Eime8a oloi entos tou mellontos mias polusun8eths shmaias pou kratei tous ex8rikous stolous empros sta teixh ths kardias mou katoxurwnontes yeudais8hseis pistopoiountes endiameses paraklhtikes metarru8miseis xwris na noh8h to antikeimenon ths palhs. Stigmiotupa mas apedei3an thn or8othta ths poreias mas pros ton proponhthn tou idiou fantasmatos ths proeleusews twn oneirwn kai tou ka8enos katoikou ths kardias mias pampalaias polhs. Otan e3antlh8oun ta xronika mas 8a fanoume gumnoteroi kai apo thn afi3i ths katadikhs paromoiwn plokamiwn kai pastrikwn varoulkwn giati oloi mas eime8a entos ths siwphs tou krhmnizomenou ponou sta gargara texnasmata tou mellontos mas. 

Otan enwpion mias krhmnizomenhs xionostivados, pou peftei apo ta uyh twn orewn kai apo tous pagous twn yuxrwn ptuxwsewn tou edafous se xamhloteres plagies, h pros to va8os mias xaradras h koilados, otan enwpion mias krhmnizomenhs xionostivados enas 8eaths h enas oreivaths katexetai apo deos, h terpetai apo thn hdonhn tou epikindunou, oxi monon hxei h hxw twn ptwsewn twn xionoswrwn, apo faraggi se faraggi, kai epanalamvanei thn voh kai parateinei thn diarkeia tou patagou, ma anthxei kai mesa sta splaxna tou oreivatou kata toiouton tropon, wste na uparxh dunatoths na epekta8h dia poikilwn viwmatwn h zwh autou tou an8rwpou, apo thn zwnhn tou vorra pros mian diakekaumenhn zwnhn, eis thn opoian na hmporh na ais8an8h autos poson polutimh ka8istatai h zesth, h zesth pou mesa ths to atomon aporrofa ola ekeina ta stoixeia, pou kapote 8a e3atmis8oun me thn seira twn, en wra anagkhs antistrofou, en wra pou to atomon epi8umei ek neou, an oxi to yuxos tou vorra, toulaxiston mian droseran pnohn anemou, mian zeidwron pnohn ek tou pelagous, pou n' anemizh ta mallia mias korhs, mias korhs, pou enw 8a skuvh ton Aprilh ston e3wsth, 8a euxetai na idh (strefousa grhgora thn kefalhn ths pros ta opisw) na plhsiazh autos - toutestin o 8eaths, toutestin o oreivaths - kai na thn pianh apo thn meshn, ws erasths h ws suzugos ths. 

8ampos o dromos thn augh, xwris skies| lampros san hxos kitrinos pneustwn to meshmeri me ton hlio. Ta antikeimena, ta ktismata stilpna kai h plasis olh me panhguri moiazei, xaroumenh mesa sto fws, san peteinos pou s' enan fraxth alalazei.
   Amerimnos o dromos e3akolou8ei, san kapoios pou sfurizontas (aeras ths anoi3ews se kalamies) amerimnos diavainei, kai oso enteinetai to fws, h kinhsis twn diavatwn, pezwn kai epoxoumenwn, ston dromo au3anei kai plh8ainei.
   Oi diavatai ametrhtoi. Anamesa se agnwstous poihtas kai agious anwnumous, anamesa se forthga diadromwn megalwn, oloi, astoi kai proletarioi diavainoun, oloi upakouontes se kati, se kati suxna polu kala maskaremeno (toutestin upakouontes sthn Moira) alloi pezoi kai alloi metakinoumenoi me troxofora, me oxhmata loghs-loghs, troxhlata poikila, mes' sthn voh diavainontes kai thn antara, me Sitroen, me Kantillak, me Bespes kai me karra.
   O dromos, skurostrwtos h me asfalto ntumenos, apo pantou panta perna - A8hna, Mosxa, Giaroslav, Londino kai Pekino, apo thn Santa Fe nte Mpogkota kai thn Gouadalaxara, thn Sierra Mantre Oriental kai tis kordillieres, mes' apo topous ierous san tous Delfous kai thn Dwdwnh, mes' apo topous endo3ous, opws ta Salwna, opws h gefura ths Alamanas, ka8ws kai apo alla merh 3akousta, san thn kosmopoli ekeinh, pou hdupa8ws thn diasxizei o gkrizos Shkouanas.
   Omws o dromos, an kai apo pantou perna, den einai panta ths amerimnhsias h ths sunh8ous sulloghs. Kamia fora fwnes akouontai thn nukta, fwnes mias gunaikos pou andres polloi s' ena xantaki thn viazoun, h alles fores, alles fwnes - ekeino to dusoiwno paraggelma: "Ston topo !" pou megan tromon esperne mes' stis yuxes twn odoiporwn, otan maxairia astraftan kai kariofilia h gkrades, empros sta sth8h twn ta3idiwtwn, otan ston dromo auton, moira kakh tous erixne sta xeria twn lhstantartwn, pou foustanella lerh forwntas, etsi ka8ws provallane apo thn mpouka mias sphlias, me pallhkaria moiazane tou Odussea Androutsou, san natan o topos to Xani ths Gravias kai oi ta3idiwtai toutoi, stratiwtai tou Kiose Mexmet h tou Omer Bruwnh - etsi, ka8ws ap' to Pikermi 3ekinwntas, pernwntas mes' ap' thn Ntaou Pentelh, apo ton dromo auton, pros monopatia dusvata tous lordous odhgousan (3an8a paidia ths Ingkliteras pou sthn Ellada hr8ane kai agiasan) me ta xantzaria oi lhstai kentrizontas tous (w Edouarde Xermpert ! w Bainer, nte Mpoul kai Lount !) wspou na f8asoun se sigoura lhmeria, konta sth Skala tou wrwpou, stou Dhlesi ta merh, gia lutra vasilika h gia maxairi (sta Salwna sfazoun arnia kai sto Xruso kriaria) gia lutra vasilika h gia sfagh (gia des kairo pou diale3e o Xaros na me parh) enw o xeimwnas teleiwne kai zugwne h Lamprh, kai murize pantou polu to peuko, to 8umari, gia lutra vasilika h gia sfagh, (w Arvanitakh Tako ! w Arvanitakh Xrhsto ! w Gerogiannh kai maure esu Katarraxia !) gia lutra vasilika h gia sfagh, konta sth Skala tou wrwpou, stou Dhlesi ta merh.
   Kai o dromos e3akolou8ei, me analoga stoixeia kai apo pantou panta perna (Gkran Kanuon, Makrotantalon, Akrokeraunia, Andeis) apo tis ox8es tou Gouadalkivir pou olh thn Kordova potizei, apo tis ox8es tou Amour kai apo tis ox8es tou Zamvezh, o dromos apo pantou perna, sklhros, sklhrotatos pantou, toso, pou pantote antexei, sta vhmata olwn twn pezwn kai sthn trivh twn varuterwn oxhmatwn, mes' apo poleis kai xwria, vouna, uyipeda kai kampous, apo tis limnes tis Finlandikes, thn Gh tou Puros kai thn Estramadoura, ews pou 3afnou, ka8e toso, mia pinakis, mh orath para stous kaloumenous, panta emfanizetai gia ton ka8ena, opou kai an vriskontai oi ghgeneis kai oi ta3idiwtai, mia pinakis me grammata xondra kai apla pou grafei: "Terma edw. Etoimas8hte. O potamos Axerwn".
   Thn idia stigmh, opoia kai an einai h xwra, opoio kai an einai to topion, ginetai mia teleutaia Benetia m' ena Kanale Gkrante - orama panta 8eion kai twn ais8hsewn xairetismos sternos - mia teleutaia Benetia stis apova8res ths opoias gondoles maures perimenoun (phga na pw san nekrofores) kai enas peraths gondolierhs, wxros kai katisxnos ma dunatos sta mpratsa, tous termatizontas ka8e fora kalei: "Peraste, kurioi, ap' edw. Touth einai h varka sas. Empate." Kai oi kaloumenoi, me vlemma san auto pou sunanta kaneis sta matia twn katadikasmenwn, stis ustates stigmes tou viou twn, mprosta stis kannes twn apospasmatwn, se wres or8rines kata tas ekteleseis, miso lepto prin akous8oun oi toufekies kai swrias8oun sfadazonta sth gh ta swmata twn, oloi pernoun kai mpainoun stis gondoles panta xwris aposkeues kai feugoun.
   Kai o dromos e3akolou8ei, sklhros, sklhroteros para pote, skurostrwtos h me asfalto ntumenos, kai malakwnei mono, opoia kai an einai h xwra, opoio kai an einai to topion, katw apo selas aglaon a8anasias, monon sta vhmata twn poihtwn ekeinwn, pou oi yuxes twn ena me ta kormia twn einai, twn poihtwn ekeinwn twn akraifnwn kai twn axrantwn, ka8ws kai twn adelfwn autwn Agiwn Pantwn.

Einai alh8es oti h plhrhs mona3ia einai vareia kai oti h erhmos einai auxmhra kai talanizei. Alla, alla, ou mhn alla (opws tou Islam to Il Alla, twn xristianwn to Exei o 8eos kai twn a8ewn ai uyhlai ai skeyeis) kaneis idrws, kamia diya, den e3antloun ton mustikon Eufrathn, pou kai en th erhmw akomh, kai entos kai peran ths sighs, entos kai peran pashs mona3ias kai pashs memyimoirias, potizei ta panta, pantote, xwris na fainetai h phgh tou, opws to mega fws, to aktiston, fwtizei ta panta eis ton aiwna, xwris na fainetai h estia, ta panta, ta panta, akomh kai ta pio mikra, oson kai to ekstatikon, to anesperon, to mega paflazon Sumpan. 

Gluka 8roizoun gurw mou ta dendra. Ti uyhlos kai ai8rios pou einai o ouranos! Mes' sthn yuxh mou to ouranion to3on kai sthn kardia mou mesa - stilpnos, pasixaros korudallos - lalei o mikros mou gios. 


Se wrismenous topous onomazoun ta xeria xeres. Sta Akrokeraunia petoun gupaetoi. Stis panwsies sourwnei h 8alassa kai anagalliazei. Stis anoiktes plateies ta paidia petoun ton Marth xrwmatistous aetous apo xarti.
            Kokkinoi, prasinoi, kitrinoi kai kapote galazioi, oi xartinoi aetoi lusikomoi kai me makries oures, petoun epanw apo thn poli, opws epanw apo thn fterh twn uyhlwn vounwn oi aetoi.
            E kstatika uywnoun ta paidia ta xeria. Deixnoun tous xartinous komhtes me tis makrues oures. Ouranioi drakoi pio yhla ta aeroplana, vrontoun kai grafoun sto sterewma me asprous kapnous tis le3eis:
KALA LE ONA NOLA PY.
            E inai h wra katasprh| h ekstasis galazia. H polis axnizei apo hdonh. Kounoun tis xeres ta paidia kai, akoma, apo ta stomata twn phdoun san pidakes oi le3eis:
KALA LE ONA NOLA PY.

Otan ustera apo thn anarxia pou'xen antariasei ton topo dinontas eis ola ta kaka stoixeia to eleutero na pra3oun ka8e loghs anomia, h ta3h eixe pale sterew8ei, k' eixe do8ei amnhstia stous kakourgous, totes epistrefan toutoi ap' ta vouna ki apo ta 3ena sta spitia tous, ki anamesa stous allous pou 3anarxontan, egurize sto xwrio tou ki o Magouladiths Antwnhs Koukouliwths.
      Eitoun totes ws saranta xronwn, kontos, mauridernos, m' omorfa pukna sgoura genia kai me sgourotata maura mallia. To proswpo tou eixe xarh kai to vlemma tou eitoun xa ideutiko kai hmero agkala ki antifegge me prasines analampes| to stoma tou omws eitoun mikrotato kai konto dixws xeilia.
      O an8rwpos toutos, prin akoma rempeleyoun o kosmos, eixe pantreutei. Ki otan phre twn vounwn to dromo, gia to fovo ths e3ousias, afhke th gunaika tou monh sto spiti kai touth den tou esta8h pisth, alla me allon (nomizontas isws pws o Koukouliwths eitoun skotwmenos h alliws pe8amenos) eixe piasei erwta ki ap' ton erwta touton eixe gennh8ei paidi pou a3ainen wstoso xaritwmena kai pou h gunaika persa agapouse.
      Egurize loipon o lhsths sto xwrio tou thn wra opou vafoun ta nera. K' emphke 3afnws spiti tou xwris kaneis na to prosmenei, emphke sa 8anatiko, anapantexa teleia, k' ekatatroma3en h atuxh gunaika, etroma3e toso, pou, pairnontas to 3an8o ths paidi sthn agkalia, to'sfigge sta sth8ia ths tremamenh, etoimh na ligo8umhsei kai xwris na dunatai na proferei le3h kamia.
      Alla o Koukouliwths pikra xamogelwntas ths eipe:
      "Mh fovasai gunaika. De sou kanw kanena kako, agkala kai sou prepoun. Einai to paidi touto diko sou; Nai; Ma oxi diko mou! Me poion, lege, to'xeis kamei;"
      T' apokri8h ekeinh louxtoukiwntas.
      "Antwnh, tipote de mporw na sou krouyw. To ftaisma mou einai megalo. Ma, to 3erw, k' h egdikhsh sou 8a'nai megalh| k' egw, adunato meros, kai to nhpio touto, pou apo to fovo tremei, de dunomaste na s' antreieutoume. Koita pws h tromara me klonizei ka8ws se thrw. Kame apo me o,ti 8eleis, ma luphsou to atuxo plasma pou den exei prostasia."
      Ka8ws emilousen h gunaika eskoteiniazen h oyh tou alla den thn antikovge. Etswpase ligo k' epeita ths eipe:
      "Gunaika kakh! Den rwtw twra oude sumvoulh sou, oude se lupoumai, oude to lupoumai. T' onoma ekeinou 8elw. Ese de 8a se peira3w. De mologas to; 8a to ma8w| to xwrio olo gnwrizei me poion ezouses kai totes 8a 8usiasw kai tous treis sas, 8a plunw th ntroph poxw lavei apo sas, plasmata atima!"
      Emolohse. Ki o Koukouliwths evghke amesws. Ki afou ustera apo wra 3anamphke sto spiti, evrhke th gunaika ston idio topon asaleuth me t' apokoimismeno tekno sthn agkalh| ton anantranize. Ma autos e3aplw8h kata ghs kai sa xortatos ekoimh8h upnon va8un ws to 3hmerwma.
      Thn allhn hmeran afou e3upnhsan ths eipe.
      "8a pame sta xthmata mas na idw mh kai keina mou'xoun arpa3ei, ka8ws mou'xe parei kai se o skotwmenos."
      "Ton skotwses!"
      Thn hmeran ekeinhn o hlios den efanh sthn Anatolh giati o ouranos eitoun gnefia giomatos kai to fws meta vias eplh8aine.
      Ki o Koukouliwths vanontas ftiari kai tsapi ston wmo ediata3e th gunaika na ton akolou8hsei mazi me to paidi ths, k' etsi evghkan k' oi treis apo to spiti.
      Kai ftanontas eis to xwrafi pou eitoun polu notero akoma apo thn prwtuternh vroxh, o lhsths eval8h na skayei lakko.
      Den eproferne le3h kai to proswpo tou eitoun xlwmo kai o idros, pou evrexe to metwpo tou, evgaine kruos. To staxti fws pou epefte apo ton ourano exrwmatize para3ena ton topo| to xinopwro thn aughn ekeinhn elegen olh tou th 8liyh. H gunaika ekoitaze periergh ki anhsuxh kai to paidaki epaignidouse me ta goulia kai me ta xwmata pou anaskaften o kakourgos. K' efanh gia mia stigmhn o hlios k' exruswse ta 3an8a mallia tou nhpiou pou aggelika xamogelouse.
      Ki wstoso o lakkos eitoun etoimos, ki o Koukouliwths, akoumpwntas sto ftuari, eipe ths gunaikos tou: 
      "Bal'to pistoma mesa".

Eitan nuxta va8ia ki afeggarh| h ghs anadine akoma zesta apo thn olohmerh kayh tou Alwnariatikou hliou| panou stes elies etrilizan adiakopa ta tridonia, kai kapou kapou akouotoun tou gkionh to lalhma. Sthn katoikia tou o Sta8hs Plakidas agrupnouse. Akoumpismenos sto katwfli tou kaluviou tou, 3upolutos kai 3emanikwtos, ekapnize upomonetika prosmenontas| mesa to kaluvi eitan adeio kai skotadero.
      "Sta8h" ton ekra3e mia fwnh tapeinh.
      "Afenth" apokri8hke amesws "kalhspera| kopiase". K' eshkw8hke me mias sianontas to platovraki tou. Epeita evgale spi8es apo ena strinari, anaye sthn isxna ena diafokeri kai me touto to mikro fanaraki, pou ekremotoun sto 8urofullo kai pou ta gualia tou eitan lugdiasmena apo to ladi kai maura apo thn a8alh.
      Sto ligo fws efanhke h morfh tou xwriath| eitan yhlos kai xontrokamwtos, misokopos sta xronia, dixws genia, alla me mikro staxti moustaki, k' eitan kakoftiasmena ta pi8emata tou makroulou proswpou tou.
      "Kalhspera Sta8h" tou 'pe o allos, enas neos omorfos, ntumenos me fragkika kala foremata kai me xamhlh ya8a sto kefali "hr8e apoye;"
      "3eflizei" apologh8hke me ponhro xamogelo "mazi me tes alles gunaikes, ekei katou st' alwni| na h fwtia pou tous feggei| akou kai to tragoudi tous. Olh mera e8erizame shmera. De sou 'pa pws den exeis na metaniwseis giati mou 'ri3es th filia sou;"
      "8a to idoume" apanthse sovara o neos| etsi mou 'lege ki o allos stes arxes. Exortase kala kala kai twra me maxetai". 
      "Kai tone fovasai;"
      "To 8eo monaxa fovoumai".
      Mia stigmh etswpasan| o neos eka8ise apanou s' ena gogguli 3ero, ediplwse ta podia tou ki akoumphse sto fraxth tou kaluviou. O Sta8hs ton ekoita3e sullogismenos kai tou 'pe:
      "Katevainw st' alwni| mhn anhsuxas an arghsei| prepei na 'vrw tropo gia na thne steilw".
      Kai afou eprofere touta ta logia, ekatevase ta matia ntropiasmenos k' ephre ton kathforo mesa sta skotadia tou elaiwna.
      "8a 'nai telos dikh mou" eipe me to nou tou o allos "as paei kai to kefali| extikiasa toson kairo twra".



      O Sta8hs Plakidas eftake se ligo st' alwni. Eitan ena siadi 3efwto trogurismeno apo elies mikrokormes. Mia fwtia kremamenh s' ena klwnari ekaie kapnizontas| s' ena meros eitan mia stoiva astakia mparmparostarou, pou pente gunaikes, ka8oumenes xamou mesa sta flikoura kai ta genia, me kalamenies 3ouvles t' anoigan, ta gumnwnan apo to floudi, k' etsi pastremena ta 'rixnan mesa s' ena yhlo tertiko. Akouontas ta pathmata tou Sta8h, parmenes kiolas apo ton kopo kai thn agrupnia, oi douleutres eixan payei to tragoudi tous| ki autos afou tes esimwse, e3efutilise prwta th fwtia pou anadwke amesws persoterh lamyh, kai, vlepontas epeita pws to tertiko eitan giomato ws to xeilo, t' adra3e paramaskala kai t' adeiase st' alwni, opou eitan ki alla polla 3efloudismena astakia.
      "Nustazete" tes erwthse fernontas opisw sth mesh to kofini| "giati den tragoudate allo; Kouragio| aurio thn augh sas skolainw nwris apo to 8ero, kai koimosaste oso 8elete to meshmeri| th nuxta pali 8a 3eflizoume".
      "Oxi de nustazoume" apanthse xasmourizontas mia nea pantremenh, pou thn elegan Leniw "ma to stoma mas estiye apo to lege-lege kai to fahto tou t' apoyino eitan nostimo kai piperato| diyoume".
      "Pollhwra se prosmenoume, Sta8h" tou 'pe h gunaika tou h Mar8a, xwriatissa proesth "gia na pioume".
      "K' evariosoune na 'r8eis apanou h idia;" ths apanthse.
      "Etsi eixes diata3ei tou logou sou" tou apologh8hke sa na '8ele na ton peira3ei.
      "Den to '3era pws o mastrapas 8a adeiaze toso glhgora" eipe o Sta8hs adiaforos "pou einai tos;" Oi gunaikes oles egureyan paspateuta t' aggeio mesa sta mparmparoflouda kai to 'vrhkan amesws| ki o Sta8hs koitazontas thn plio nea, kopela dekoxtw xronwn, m' eugenika sousoumia kai paxoulh, ths eipe: - "3alafrwse esu, Stalaxth, th gerontissa mou| aneva sto kaluvi| to 3udi, 3ereis, einai sto mpoth, kai to nero sthn 3esta".
      H kopela eshkw8hke amesws mhxanika etina3e to forema ths, ephre to mastrapa, k' ekinhse kata ton anhforo. Kai den eixe alargeyei polu, otan h gria Mar8a, san na upoyiaze kati, anastena3e va8ia, k' etragoudhse touthn th rimna paraponetika:

      Polu yhla ekames fwlia kai 8a sou geirei o klwnos
      kai 8a sou pesei to pouli kai 8a sou meinei o ponos.

      Oi alles treis gunaikes me mia fwnh esunodeyan to tragoudi ths.
      "Giati to lete auto;" erwthse o Sta8hs anhsuxos.
      "Giati" apokri8hke mia kopela "h Stalaxth exei agaph me to prwto kefali tou xwriou mas".
      "Kai 8a gelastei" eprostese sovara h Leniw.
      "Kai me poione;" erwthse o Sta8hs deixnontas periergeia.
      "O kosmos to 'xei voukino k' emeis kroufo kamari" apologh8hke peiraxtika h Mar8a "legete to eleutera| h na to pw egw kallio| me ton kur Giwrgh ton Artemh, pou o pateras tou ka8etai sth xwra".
      O Sta8hs thn ekoita3e lo3a, alla den thn apophre. 3afnws akousthkan pathmata an8rwpou podemenou, pou erxotoun viastikos| k' eprose3e. O an8rwpos esimwse kai sto fws tou luxnariou ton egnwrise amesws| eitan o Giannhs o Lakouras, enas neos yhlos kai kalokamwmenos, 3an8omallhs kai 3an8ogenhs. Toutos sovaros ekalhsperise| kai ton antixairethsan prosmenontas anupomona to mantato| ekoita3e tes gunaikes mia mia k' erwthse deila: - "De douleuei dw k' h Stalaxth;"
      "Nai" apokri8hkan oles me mia fwnh.
      "Kai pou einai;" eipe vraxna.
      "Paei gia pioto sto kaluvi".
      O Giannhs ekatevase to skoteiniasmeno proswpo tou k' esta8hke skeftikos sa na '8ele na parei sovarhn apofash, ma o Sta8hs amesws ekatalave pws ta rwthmata tou den eitan a8wa, ki apotoma tou 'pe: - "Ti se mellei;"
      "Me mellei" apanthse anastenazontas| tes kopeles tou xwriou tes ferneis edw gia na tes xaneis apo ton kosmo;"
      "Panagia voh8a" efwna3an 3afnismenes oi treis gunaikes oi 3enes sa na tes aggize autes o logos tou Giannh.
      "Giati vrizeis to spiti mas;" tou fwna3e h Mar8a, pou 8umwmenh eixe shkw8ei or8h.
      "Sto kaluvi sas einai ki o gios tou Artemh, ton akolou8hsa apo to xwrio" apokri8hke ayiwmenos.
      "8e mou ! ti lhsteia kai ti katafronia" ekaman oi gunaikes xtupwntas ta sth8ia tous ki arxisan na klaine.
      Ma o Sta8hs tou 'pe agroika: - "Auta ta kaneis giati s' e3empourise apo to spiti tou| ton h8eles kleismenon, xwris gnwres me to xwrio tou, gia na kaneis esu to megalone me ta ovola tou| pane twra auta, lhsmonhse ta".
      "Tou 'fuga giati oi vrwmodouleies de m' aresoun| ma mou kanei tosh luph ekeinh h dustuxismenh".
      "Oute autos, oute 'gw de se fovomaste". 
      "De 8a sas vgei se kalo| 8a idoume ti a3izete oi kainourioi oi filoi". K' etsi legontas ekame kinhma n' anevei ton anhforo.
      "Pou pas;" tou fwna3e o Sta8hs "oi gioi mou 8a se varesoun ntoufekia kai 8a pas sa skulos| tetoia wra den peirazoun ta spitia". K' esfouri3e dunata.
      "Kakourge" tou 'kra3e o Giannhs gurizontas opisw| "einai apanou o Artemhs"| k' exa8hke mesa sta skotadia tou elaiwna. 
      "Ti ekames, Sta8h, apoye" eipe h Mar8a klaiontas opws k' oi alles gunaikes| "kallio na xalouses monasthri".
      "8e mou, 8e mou !" eipan 8rhnwntas oi alles.


      Eixe er8ei h mera| sthn katoikia tou Sta8h Plakida oi pente gunaikes, amilhtes kai luphmenes, e8erizan ta 3an8a t' astakia tou mparmparostarou| ena ena ta 'koftan apo ta 3era kalamia tous, esunazan kamposa sto anashkwmeno forema tous, - pou m' ena xeri to kratousan sa saki - k' epeita erxontan kai t' adeiazan mesa sta yhla tertika. O idios o Sta8hs epairne ta kofinia paramaskala otan eitan giomata, ta 'ferne st' alwni k' eswriaze to gennhma sth stiva. Ma out' autos den elege logo. K' epernasan etsi oi droseres wres ths aughs.
      Eitan o hlios yhla, otan sto xwrafi eparousiasthke o 8anashs o Maravas, o pateras ths Stalaxths, enas xwriaths skevrwmenos apo ta xronia kai th dustuxia, kakontumenos, mikroswmos ki adunatos. To proswpo tou eitan liwmeno apo th luph, k' ekratouse to vlemma katevasmeno apo th ntroph. O Sta8hs erixthke gia na tone dextei kai ton odhghse ston iskio sima st' alwni| epaskise na tou xamogelasei xairetwntas ton, ma o geros den tou apanthse.
      "Tou ta 'pe ola o Lakouras" esullogisthke k' eprosmeine na milhsei prwtos o allos.
      Oi gunaikes 8erizontas tous ekoitazan.
      "Ti ema8ame" eipe se ligo o 8anashs xwris na shkwsei to mati tou pou estaze| "gi' auto sou th steilame thn kakomoira; Eisai Ioudas !"
      "Den esta8hke tipota" tou apokri8hke ntropiasmenos| "mhn akous ta yemata| mono hr8e edw th nuxta o Giwrghs o Artemhs| rwta tes gunaikes".
      Mia axtida elpidas efe3e st' aulakwmeno metwpo tou gerontou| etolmhse na shkwsei to kefali| k' ekoita3e to Sta8h katamata. Toutos ekokkinhse sugxusmenos.
      "Iouda" tou 'pe o 8anashs axnizontas persotero. K' epeita estrafhke pros tes gunaikes k' ekra3e th 8ugatera tou, pou amesws ton upakouse. Eitan axnh k' ekeinh, k' eixe ta matia prhsmena kai kokkina kai t' axeili marameno.
      "Eisai xamenh" ths eipe apelpismenos.
      Auth eval8hke amesws na klaiei.
      "Den ein' etsi" eipe o Sta8hs zwera| "lege thn alh8eia, Stalaxth| o pateras sou de 8elei na me pisteyei".
      "Xamenh den eimai" apokri8hke sfouggizontas ta dakrua me thn akrh ths mpolias ths| "giati m' agapaei. Apo ta persi to panhguri tou ah-Lios, opou mazi exoreyame, m' evale, leei, sthn kardia tou| kai 8a me parei, leei, kai tou to pisteuw. Mou orkisthke, me to xeri apanou sthn eikona ths Panagias sou, Sta8h, pws 8a me stefanwsei| alliws den ton afhna na m' agkaliasei".
      "Ti ekames;" ths eipe o pateras me megalon pono| k' aistan8hke pws ta podia tou adunatizan, pws ta gonata tou ekovontan k' eka8ise kata ghs gia na mhn pesei. H ntroph ton ekurieue, ekrouye to proswpo tou mesa stes palames tou k' eklaige me parapono.
      "Stalaxth" ekame o Sta8hs epeita apo ligo "emena de mou 'pes etsi".

      Mia stigmh etswpasan k' oi treis tous, k' epeita o Sta8hs stenoxwremenos eipe: - "O,ti eginhke de dior8wnetai| as koita3oume na voleutoun ta pramata, kai na glutwsei kai touth."
      "Pws;" erwthse o gerontas kounwntas pikra to kefali| "touth den exei tipota ston kosmo| giati k' ekeino pou 'xe ws extes, thn timh ths, ths thn ephre". K' eval8hke pali na klaiei.
      "Mhn kaneis etsi" tou apanthse o allos me splaxnos| "pame na vroume ton kur Giwrgh kai na tou milhsoume".
      "Pame n' akousw ki apo ta xeilh tou thn katadikh ths. Einai gia pni3imo, h kakomoira". K' etsi legontas ekame dunamh tou eautou tou k' eshkw8hke.
      Ki authn thn stigmh tous esimwse tou Sta8h h gunaika pou epeta3e th mpolia ths apo to kefali k' eipe 8rhnhtika: - "Ti kako mas eplakwse, Sta8h, me touthn th dustuxismenh".
      O antras ths ths eri3e mia lo3h matia, k' ekinhse mazi me to geronta.


      Anevhkan sto Murtero, to xwrio tous, k' ediavainan twra apo to megalo dromo. Ekane zesta pollh| o hlios erixne apo yhla tes purwmenes axtides tou pou epeftan st' asprismena spitia kai ta 'kanan n' anadinoun kaya k' ekeina. Oi diavates eitan spanioi kai liga argasthria anoixta. Ma s' ena, tou Gerodhmou, sto kentrikotero meros tou xwriou, eixe sunaxtei kamposos kosmos. Ekei8es epernousan twra o Sta8hs me ton patera ths Stalaxths k' eidan pws autou mesa emilouse megalofwna kai anhsuxa o Giannhs o Lakouras, fanera gia to genomeno ths nuxtos. K' eitan h omilia tou ayia kai thn esuntrofeue me xeronomies tragikes kai suxna anemize kai th maggoura tou pou thn ekremouse epeita apo to guristari sto vraxioni tou ! Kai ton akouan oloi prosextikoi k' epainousan me kounhma tou kefaliou ta logia tou, koitazontas o enas ton allon.
      O Sta8hs eglhgoreye to pathma tou k' etravh3e apo to maniki to geronta| ma wstoso o Giannhs tous eixe idei apo mesa kai 3afnws epaye thn kouventa tou k'epetaxthke sto dromo kai tous estamathse. Oi a8rwpoi pou eitan sto magazi eshkw8hkan apo ta ka8isthria tous k' ekoitazan apo thn porta kai ta para8ura.
      "S' epiase touth h alwpou" efwna3e o Giannhs tou 8anash, sfiggontas ta dontia| "alla sou 'pa ki alla kaneis".
      "Metra ta logia sou" ekame o Sta8hs me sovaron tropo k' etravh3e pali to geronta.
      "Ti prosmeneis akoma;" erwthse opisw o Giannhs empodizontas tous na proxwresoun.
      "8a koita3w to kako na mh genei xeirotero" apanthse o 8anashs anastenazontas| "Prwta 8a idw na vre8ei dior8wmos".
      "Kai ti dior8wmos; Bale fwtia sta megala ta spitia ! H ftwxeia 8a zhsete kalutera." K' etsi legontas o Giannhs me to maggouri tou efoverize thn korfh mianhs raxhs, opou efainotoun ena spiti kaloxtismeno, kleismeno gurou me toixous kai me yhla kuparisia, pou eprovalan apanw8e tous, kounwntas analafra edw k' ekei tis muteres korfes tous.
      "Den to kanw| 8a xasw kai thn yuxh mou" tou apokri8hke o 8anashs xamhlofwna.
      "Tou prepei omws. Kai 8a' vlepes kai toutounous tous mesatores na yofoun ths peinas, opws prwta pou den eitan stou Artemh."
      Etsi eipe o Giannhs k' eitan xaziri na milhsei akoma| alla apo mesa, apo to magazi, akousthke h fwnh tou noikokurh, enou paxiou, sovarou xwriath, polege: - Exei dikio o gerontas| as koita3ei na dior8wsei to prama. Ti 8a kerdisei me ta fonika;"
      O kosmos epainese to logo ki o Giannhs eparamerise, tous afhke na fugoun k' emphke pali sto magazi.



      Se mia megalh kamara tou spitiou tou o Giwrghs Artemhs eperpatouse apanou katou anhsuxos, otan emphke o Sta8hs mesa. "Ti trexei;" erwthse amesws o neos stamatwntas kai dixws na kalhmerisei.
      "8elei na se idei ths kopelos o pateras" tou apokri8hke taragmenos "einai katou sthn kourth sou, ta3e tou o,ti mporeseis, giati o allos anastatwnei to xwrio".
      "As er8ei" eipe skeftikos o Artemhs| k' enw o Sta8hs evgaine sto para8uro gia na fwna3ei to geronta, eprostese milwntas monaxos tou: "Kahmenh Stalaxth, ti na kamw gia na mou s' afhsoun;"
      "Anevainei" eipe o Sta8hs, ka8izontas s' ena skamni.
      Kai se mia stigmh o gerontas eitan epanou, ki o Artemhs ton exairethse deixnontas adiaforia| ma den elave apanthsh. Me tapeino vlemma ekoitaze o adikhmenos ologura tou| e3etaze tou spitiou ta epipla pou tou efainontan a3etimwta, esunomoiaze me to nou tou ekeino to palati me th ftwxh katoikia tou k' ekrine pws eitan adunato, gia th megalh koinwnikh diafora, na pathsei h 8ugatera tou autou mesa. To proswpo tou edei3e pali aperanth luph kai to vlemma tou eproshlw8hke xamou.
      "Geronta de mileis;" erwthse o Sta8hs gia na diakoyei thn anupoferth siwph.
      "Ti na pw;" apologh8hke me to kefali katou| "autos prepei na milhsei, uster' ap' o,ti ekame".
      O Artemhs ton ekoita3e 3etastika kai me yuxoponoia k' ekatalave th megalh pikra tou an8rwpou pou h fusikh adunamia kai h tapeinwsh tou thn ediplwne| ton esimwse kai deixnontas tou ena ka8isma tou 'pe:
      "Mh stoxazesai pws den agapaw thn kopela;"
      "An thn agapouses de 8a thn ekakomoiriazes" tou apokri8hke xwris na kounh8ei "ma o 8eos timwraei thn adikia".
      "Mh 8umwneis" tou 'pe o Sta8hs "den kerdizeis tipota. Ti 8eleis; Lege to 3astera".
      "Na thn parei" apanthse apofasistika k' ekoita3e gurw tou san 3afnismenos apo to logo tou.
      "Gureueis to adunato" apanthse o Sta8hs me sovaroth.
      Ma o 8anashs den tou apologh8hke| eprosmene, xlwmos apo th luph kai thn amfivolia, thn apofash tou Artemh| kai toutos aistan8hke mesa tou thn anagkh na pranei ton adikhmenon kai na ton euxaristhsei, esullogisthke kiolas t' anakatwmata sto xwrio, thn kakoglwssia tou Lakoura, to xamo ths agaphmenhs tou| k' eskefthke kiolas pws ola edunotoun na ta hsuxasei kai na ta dior8wsei enas tou monos logos pou emporouse kai na ton a8ethsei san erxotoun h volikh stigmh.
      "Einai o skopos mou" eipe kokkinizontas. "Mou th dineis;"
      Tou gerontou to ponemeno proswpo elamye me mias apo xara| to mati tou eplhmmurise dakrua kai ligwmenos apo th sugkinhsh eka8ise. -"To leei h tuxh ths" eipe epeita apo liges stigmes "na mpei edw mesa;" Kai sa na mhn pisteue erwthse: - "To 3ereis kur Giwrgh, h kopela einai ftwxia polu".
      "To gnwrizw" apokri8hke xamhlofwna sa na ntrepotoun.
      "Ki o afenths o pateras sou ti 8a pei;" 3anarwthse o geros.
      "8a ta kataferw egw| 8a idei kai thn peristash| kai pali an den metapeistei pairnoume alla metra".
       O 8anashs emeine mia stigmh siwphlos, ananoh8hke pws oute h pantreia den esvhne teleiwtika to ntropiasma ths 8ugateros tou, ki anastena3e: - "Afou thn h8eles" eipe "giati den thn egureues prwta;"
      "To kamwmeno den 3egenetai" apokri8hke o Sta8hs.
      "Einai alh8eia" eipe o gerontas kounwntas to kefali kai ta matia tou edakrusan. "Sou dinw thn eukh mou san paidiou mou" eprostese sugkinhmenos. K' elhsmonhse me mias th luph tou| to proswpo tou eginhke xaroumeno, to adunato kormi tou to aistan8hke 3ananiwmeno k' eixe viash na khru3ei tou kosmou thn anepantexh tuxh ths Stalaxths tou, to lampro sunoikesio. "Phgainw" 3akolou8hse "na ths t' anaferw| w poso 8a xarei kai keinh !"
      K' eshkw8hke gia na fugei| k' eshkw8hke ki o Sta8hs gia na tou paei katopi. - "Mh lhsmonhseis" tou 'pe "pws prepei na mas keraseis olous sto xwrio, afou ekames tetoia pantreia".
      "Nai" apokri8hke k' ekinhsan.
      Ki o Giwrghs Artemhs, monaxos tou twra, e3anaval8hke na perpatei apanou katou sto megalo dwmatio tou anhsuxos, zugiazontas to megalo logo pou 'xe proferei, k' eipe monologwntas: "Etsi den to 'xa sullogistei| eparaviasthka isws| panta o klefths einai kai yeuths".


      St' argasthri tou Gerodhmou o Giannhs o Lakouras edhmhgorouse panta me thn idian ayioth. Omws otan eide na 'rxontai oi duo etswpase 3afnws k' edagkase peismwmenos ta xeilia tou parathrwntas th xaroumenhn oyh tous. Toutoi emphkan st' argasthri, o 8anashs eka8ise epishma mpros s' ena trapezi k' eipe tou noikokurh:
      "Bale piota gia olous| thne pairnei".
      Osoi eitan autou ton ekoita3an 8iamazontas k' emeinan statikoi mh vriskontas ta prepoumena logia gia tetoion eutuxismo, mono to proswpo tou Giannh esugneye persotero. Me vraxnh fwnh tou 'pe pikramenos: - "Se gelaei| de 8a to kamei pote| oi goneoi tou de 8' afhsoun| kai su 8a meineis me thn ntroph, kakomoirh| tou 'prepe skotwma !"
      "Paralogas, Giannh", tou apanthse o argasthriarhs sovaros "afou 8elei na dior8wsei to sfalma tou, giati na mh genei o gamos;"
      "Swsta, swsta" eipe olos o kosmos| kai pinontas ta rakia, pou wstoso o Gerodhmos ta 'xe etoimasei, esugxairontan to 8anash.
      Kai o Sta8hs enohse pws arese tou kosmou h apofash tou Artemh, k' eskefthke: - "Twra einai h stigmh gia na xasei o Lakouras oshn upolhyh tou 'xoun". Amesws evghke apo t' argasthri, anevhke trexatos sto spiti tou Artemh kai se ligo e3anar8e mazi tou.
      wstoso oi a8rwpoi epinan xaroumenoi| erwtousan periergoi to 8anash gia ta ka8ekasta tou sunapanthmou tou me ton Artemh, h8elan na ma8oun pote 8a genotoun h xara, mono o Lakouras eka8otoun se mian akrh xwris na krenei oute logo kai den eshkw8hke otan emphke o Artemhs.
      Oi alloi oloi ton edexthkan me sevas, kai ton eukiontan apo kardias. - "Na 'ste poluxronoi" tou 'legan "poluxronoi". Kai tou 'kaman topo na ka8isei sth mesh tous.
       Autos eparaggeile krasi gia olous k' e3anoige me to mati pou eitan o Lakouras| antamwse to vlemma tou, pou eitan giomato meyh kai ton eide pws eshkwnotoun gia na fugei. Sima sth mpasia evre8hkan antimetwpoi| to aima tous evraze.
      "Giati me vrizeis shmera olh mera sto foro;" erwthse apofasistika o Artemhs.
      "Giati sou prepei" tou apokri8hke agroika "etsi kanoun oi timioi; tetoian kopela, tou xwriou thn kaluterh, na thn katanteseis s' auth th 8esh;"
      Ma o kosmos akouontas anakatw8hke kakofxaristhmenos apo to malwma ki o noikokurhs tou argasthriou eipe didaxtika: - "Exeis adiko shmera, Giannh| o kur Giwrghs, ki an esfale, edior8wse to la8os| kai na, ths kopelos o pateras krazetai euxaristhmenos. Phgaine sto kalo twra".
      "Timia tou milhse" eipan polloi epainwntas.
      Ma o Artemhs eixe 8umwsei kai den afhne to diava eleutero: - "K' exeis xreos esu" eipe megalofwna tou Giannh "na m' elegxeis, esu pou toson kairo etrwges to ywmi mou;"
      "Afontis thn epeira3es sou 'fuga."
      "yema ! s' ediw3a, giati de se skiazomai| paei o kairos pou 'vanes nomo sto xwrio."
      Ta matia tou Lakoura astrayan, sa na 'xe parei mesa tou megalhn apofash, ma o Artemhs to katalave| m' ormh tou phre to maggouri kai tou 'pe: - "Egw o idios 8a se timwrhsw, ywmopath". K' etsi legontas anemise to 3ulo gia na tou to ferei katakefala kai parathrhse pws kanenas den ekouniotoun gia na uperaspisei to Giannh| 3afnws omws alla3e gnwmh, ekrine kalutero na katafronesei ton oxtro tou para na ton xtuphsei k' epellhse to palouki o3w apo thn porta. "De se katadexomai, fuge !" tou 'pe.
      O allos axnise| efere mhxanika to xeri sth zwsh, gia na vgalei t' armata tou, ma h skeyh den ton afhke na to kamei: - "An tone skotwsw" eipe me to nou tou "8a 'xw egw to krima ths Stalaxths, kai m' olo pou 'nai xamenh kai twra, o kosmos 8a leei pws egw thn ekatestreya". Ki anastena3e| epeita ekoita3e ton Artemh katamata kai tou 'pe" - "Einai h prwth fora pou enas me vrizei dhmosia"| kai ntropiasmenos evghke apo t' argasthri.


      Eixe er8ei to karpero xinopwro| sto spiti tou 8anash eixan etoimasei ta proikia tou gamou| h Stalaxth eforouse ka8e giortasimh mera ta plousia stolidia pou ths eixe xarisei o gampros ki ontas epishma arravwniasmenh, eixe to eleutero na phgainoerxetai stou Artemh xwris na para3enofainetai kanenou. To xwrio edeixne adiaforia kai o idios o Lakouras den emilouse plia.
      Thn paramonh tou Staurou, s' ena kampo kataprasino sima sto potami, gunaikes tragoudwntas, etrugousan ta wrma stafulia st' ampelia tou Artemh. Eitan autou oi 8eristres k' oi pente: h Stalaxth, h Mar8a, h Leniw k' oi duo alles kopeles| o Sta8hs Plakidas epistatouse, evoh8ouse na fortwnoun st' aloga ta tertika pou ena ena ta giomizan oi gunaikes k' esterne ta stafulia sto xwrio me tous agwgiates. To xwrio omws eitan alarga ki o dromos kakos| exreiazotoun mia wra olakerh gia na pan kai na 'r8oun ta zwa. Eixan kamei apo thn augh tesseres strates kai twra o hlios eitan yhla k' oi axtides tou epeftan kauteres sto livadi.
      "Na fame ywmi" eipe o Sta8hs stes gunaikes "t' aloga 8' arghsoun na 3anar8oun, giati sto xwrio 8a ta tagisoun kai 8a geutoun k' oi agwgiates". K' etsi legontas hr8e sthn akropotamia k' eka8ise ston iskio mianhs megalhs leukas. Oi gunaikes ton akolou8hsan k' eka8isan kata ghs kai keines sima tou. To potami eree fliflizontas, t' ashmenia fulla tou dentrou etzitzirizan tremamena, polla poulia ekeladousan trogurou. O Sta8hs emoirase to kitrino ywmi, oi gunaikes ephran stafulia apo ta kala8ia tous ki arxisan oloi na trwgoun.
      "Einai mera nhsteyimh shmera" eipe o Sta8hs "gi' auto ywmi monato".
      "Pote na mh leiyei to vlohmeno" apokri8hke amesws h Mar8a.
      H Stalaxth emasouse skeftikh sa na eitan h kardia ths anhsuxh k' epeita apo ligo eipe tou Sta8h:
      "Erwthses tous agwgiates an hr8e;"
      "Perimenetai apo stigmh se stigmh" apologh8hke kai to metwpo tou esoufrw8hke.
      "O pe8eros sou;" thn erwthse h Mar8a anastenazontas.
      "Nai" apokri8hke h Stalaxth katevazontas ta matia "na idoume ti 8a pei| afontis me phre o gios tou den tou 'graye tipota. Ma opws ki an einai glhgora 8a me stefanwsei o kur Giwrghs| pou na m' afhkei twra thn kahmenh; Duo mhnes zoume antama".
      "Kalh sterewsh" ths eukh8hkan oi alles gunaikes| k' h Leniw eprostese: - "Akouetai omws pws o gerontas de se 8elei".
      H Stalaxth ekounhse tes plates sa na 'lege "den 3erw" k' h Mar8a ths eipe anastenazontas: - "Dolia Stalaxth".
      "Den 3eroume akoma tipota" ekame o Sta8hs katsoufiasmenos| "ma opws ki an er8oun ta pramata, esu de ftais, Stalaxth, sou eitan grammena".
      Kamia den apologh8hke| ki apofagan glhgora xwris na proferoun le3h| epeita oi gunaikes e3anar8an sto 8elhma tous, ki o Sta8hs emeine ston iskio karterwntas t' aloga.
      "Shmera einai megalh mera" ananoh8hke| "na idoume ti 8a ferei. Ma o gerontas pou na sugklinei| kai den fovoumai allon para to Lakoura| 8a 'xoume antares". K' etsi legontas e3aplw8hke kai apokoimh8hke.


      H fwnh kai to skounthma tou Artemh, pou, kavalarhs st' alogo tou, eixe katevei me tous agwgiates st' ampeli ton e3upnhsan. Mazeu8hkan oi Ale3andrinoi
na doun ths Kleopatras ta paidia,
ton Kaisariwna, kai ta mikra tou aderfia,
Ale3andro kai Ptolemaio, pou prwth
fora ta vgazan e3w sto Gumnasio,
ekei na ta khru3oun vasileis,
mes sth lamprh parata3i twn stratiwtwn.

O Ale3andros ton eipan vasilea
ths Armenias, ths Mhdias, kai twn Par8wn.
O Ptolemaios ton eipan vasilea
ths Kilikias, ths Surias, kai ths Foinikhs.
O Kaisariwn stekontan pio emprosta,
ntumenos se meta3i triantafulli,
sto sth8os tou an8odesmh apo uakin8ous,
h zwnh tou diplh seira sapfeirwn ki ame8ustwn,
demena ta podhmata tou m' aspres
kordelles kenthmenes me rodoxroa margaritaria.
Auton ton eipan piotero apo tous mikrous,
auton ton eipan Basilea twn Basilewn.

Oi Ale3andrinoi enoiw8an vevaia
pou hsan logia auta kai 8eatrika.

Alla h mera htane zesth kai poihtikh,
o ouranos ena galazio anoixto,
to Ale3andrino Gumnasion ena
8riamviko kator8wma ths texnhs,
twn aulikwn h poluteleia ektakth,
o Kaisariwn olo xaris ki emorfia
(ths Kleopatras uios, aima twn Lagidwn)|
k' oi Ale3andrinoi etrexan pia sthn eorth,
k' en8ousiazontan, k' epeufhmousan
ellhnika, k' aiguptiaka, kai poioi evraiika,
gohteumenoi me t' wraio 8eama
m' olo pou vevaia h3euran ti a3izan auta,
ti koufia logia hsane autes h vasileies. 

E pituxeis kai plhrws ikanopoihmenoi,
o vasileus Ale3andros Iannaios,
k' h suzugos tou h vasilissa Ale3andra
pernoun me proporeuomenhn mousikhn
kai me pantoian megaloprepeian kai xlidhn,
pernoun ap' tes odous ths Ierousalhm.
E telesforhse lamprws to ergon
pou arxisan o megas Ioudas Makkavaios
k' oi tessares periwnumoi adelfoi tou|
kai pou meta anendotws sunexis8h en mesw
pollwn kindunwn kai pollwn dusxereiwn.
Twra den emeine tipote to anoikeion.
Epause ka8e upotagh stous alazonas
monarxas ths Antioxeias. Idou
o vasileus Ale3andros Iannaios,
k' h suzugos tou h vasilissa Ale3andra
ka8' ola isoi pros tous Seleukidas.
Ioudaioi kaloi, Ioudaioi agnoi, Ioudaioi pistoi pro pantwn.
Alla, ka8ws pou to apaitoun h peristaseis,
kai ths ellhnikhs lalias eidhmones|
kai m'  Ellhnas kai m' ellhnizontas
monarxas sxetismenoi plhn san isoi, kai n' akouetai.
Twonti etelesforhse lamprws,
etelesforhse perifanws
to ergon pou arxisan o megas Ioudas Makkavaios
k' oi tessares periwnumoi adelfoi tou. 

E is to xrusovoullon pou evgal' o Ale3ios Komnhnos
gia na timhsei thn mhtera tou epifanws,
thn lian nohmona Kurian Anna Dalasshnh 
thn a3iologh sta erga ths, sta h8h 
uparxoun diafora egkwmiastika:
edw as metaferoume apo auta
mia frasin emorfhn, eugenikh
"Ou to emon h to son, to yuxron touto rhma, errh8h". 

Ston prologo ths Ale3iados ths 8rhnei,
gia thn xhreia ths h Anna Komnhnh.

E is iliggon ein' h yuxh ths. "Kai
rei8rois dakruwn", mas legei, "periteggw
tous of8almous..... Feu twn kumatwn" ths zwhs ths,
"feu twn epanastasewn". Thn kaiei h odunh 
"mexris ostewn kai muelwn kai merismou yuxhs".

Omws h alh8eia moiazei pou mia luph monhn
kairian egnwrisen h filarxh gunaika|
enan kaumo va8u monaxa eixe
(ki as mhn t' omologei) h agerwxh auth Graikia,
pou den katafere, m' olhn thn de3iothta ths,
thn Basileian n' apokthsei| ma thn phre
sxedon mes' ap' ta xeria ths o propeths Iwannhs. 


E 3eutelis8h plhrws.         Mia erwtikh roph tou
lian apagoreumenh         kai perifronhmenh
(emfuth molontouto)         uphr3en h aitia:
htan h koinwnia         semnotufh polu.
Exase va8mhdon         to ligosto tou xrhma|
katopi th seira,        kai thn upolhyi tou.
Plhsiaze ta trianta         xwris pote enan xrono
na vgalei se douleia,         toulaxiston gnwsth.

Kathnths' enas tupos         pou an s' evlepan mazu tou

All' oxi monon touta.         Den 8atane swsto.
A3izei parapanw         ths emorfias tou h mnhmh.
Mia apoyis allh uparxei         pou an idw8ei apo authn

kai thn upolhyi tou         e8ese ane3etastws
ths ka8arhs sarkos tou         thn ka8arh hdonh.

Ap' thn upolhyi tou;         Ma h koinwnia pou htan
semnotufh polu         susxetize kouta. 

Touto eis auton uphrxe to 3exwristo,
pou mesa s' olhn tou thn eklusi
kai thn pollhn tou peiran erwtos,
par' olhn thn sunei8ismenh tou

htan stigmes pou 8umize parado3a
efhvo pou kapws ade3ia sthn agaph

Den ta hura pia 3ana  ta toso grhgora xamena ....
ta poihtika ta matia, to xlwmo
to proswpo .... sto nuxtwma tou dromou ....

pou etsi eukola paraithsa|
kai pou katopi me agwnian h8ela.
Ta poihtika ta matia, to xlwmo to proswpo,
ta xeilh ekeina den ta hura pia. 
Mesa s' ena kivwtio h mesa s' ena epiplo apo polutimon eveno 8a valw kai 8a fula3w ta endumata ths zwhs mou.
      Ta rouxa ta kuana. Kai epeita ta kokkina, ta pio wraia auta apo ola. Kai katopin ta kitrina. Kai teleutaia pali ta kuana, alla polu pio 3e8wra auta ta deutera apo ta prwta.
      8a ta fula3w me eulaveia kai me pollh luph.
      Otan 8a forw maura rouxa, kai 8a katoikw mesa s' ena mauro spiti, mesa se mia kamarh skoteinh, 8a anoigw kamia fora to epiplo me xara, me po8o, kai me apelpisia.
      8a vlepw ta rouxa kai 8a 8umoumai thn megalh eorth - pou 8a einai tote olws diolou teleiwmenh.
      Olws diolou teleiwmenh. Ta epipla skorpismena atakta mes stes ai8ouses. Piata kai pothria spasmena kata ghs. Ola ta keria kamena ws to telos. Olo to krasi piwmeno. Oloi oi kalesmenoi feugatoi. Merikoi kourasmenoi 8a ka8ontai olomonaxoi, san k' emena, mesa se spitia skoteina - alloi pio kourasmenoi 8a phgan na koimh8oun.
Mh omileite peri enoxhs, mh omileite peri eu8unhs. Otan perna to Suntagma ths Hdonhs me mousikhn kai shmaias| otan rigoun kai tremoun ai ais8hseis, afrwn kai asevhs einai ostis menei makran, ostis den orma eis thn kalhn ekstrateian, thn vainousan epi thn katakthsin twn apolausewn kai twn pa8wn.
      Oloi oi nomoi ths h8ikhs - kakws nohmenoi, kakws efarmozomenoi - einai mhden kai den hmporoun na sta8oun oude stigmhn, otan perna to Suntagma ths Hdonhs me mousikhn kai shmaias.
      Mh afhshs kamian skieran arethn na se vasta3h. Mh pisteuhs oti kamia upoxrewsis se denei. To xreos sou einai na endidhs, na endidhs pantote eis tas Epi8umias, pou einai ta teleiotata plasmata twn teleiwn 8ewn.
