      Mh kleiesai en tw oikw sou kai planasai me 8ewrias dikaiosunhs, me tas peri amoivhs prolhyeis ths kakws kamwmenhs koinwnias. Mh leghs, Toson a3izei o kopos mou kai toson ofeilw na apolausw. Opws h zwh einai klhronomia kai den ekames tipote dia na thn kerdishs ws amoivhn, outw klhronomia prepei na einai kai h Hdonh. Mh kleiesai en tw oikw sou| alla kratei ta para8ura anoikta, oloanoikta, dia na akoushs tous prwtous hxous ths diavasews twn stratiwtwn, otan f8anh to Suntagma ths Hdonhs me mousikhn kai shmaias.
      Mh apath8hs apo tous vlasfhmous osoi se legoun oti h uphresia einai epikindunos kai epiponos. H uphresia ths hdonhs einai xara diarkhs. Se e3antlei, alla se e3antlei me 8espesias me8as. Kai epi telous otan peshs eis ton dromon, kai tote einai h tuxh sou zhleuth. Otan perash h khdeia sou, ai Morfai tas opoias eplasan ai epi8umiai sou 8a riyoun leiria kai roda leuka epi tou feretrou sou, 8a se shkwsoun eis tous wmous twn efhvoi 8eoi tou Olumpou, kai 8a se 8ayoun eis to Koimhthrion tou Idewdous opou asprizoun ta mauswleia ths poihsews.

Korh me ta xrusa mallia stous krustallenious wmous,

-Kai an xoreuoun ta stoixia, stoixia ein' as xoreuoun|

"Pisth mou, leg' o filos mou, skuye na se filhsw|

Kai pairnei vraxo kai vouno ton dromo p' anevainei,

"Poios tara3e ton upno mou; fwnazei 8umwmenh|

-Es' eisai, file, pou zhtei h agaphtikh sou;

Bou, vou, gauizoun ta skulia ki oi koukouvagies klaine,

Kai maurh thn eikona ths thn exei sthn kardia tou.

-Ax! ein' alh8eia; file mou, se 3anavlepw palai;

Ki agkaliase, kai fila me san agaphtikos mou,
Kai mein' aiwnia pistos ki aiwnia dikos mou.-

-Korh mou, einai gia filia ta xeilia maramena,
Kai gia glukagkaliasmata ta xeria mou demena.-

-Ki anisws einai gia filia ta xeilia maramena,
Ki an einai gi' agkaliasmata ta xeria sou demena,
Tot' afhse me, file mou, egw na s' agkaliasw,
Ki afou se hura mia fora, pote na mh se xasw.-

Ou! o anemostrovilos ta kuparissia dernei!
Ou! o vorias ton platano 3errizwmeno pairnei!
Kai klammata, kai ax! kai vax! mes' sth notia gruniazoun,
Kai yalmoudies mes ston voria ton uyiston do3azoun,
Kai sunnefa katamaura sfurizoune ki astraftoun,
Ki apo lampades ta vouna kai ta lagkadi' anaftoun,
Ki olo ta maura sunnefa astraftoun kai sfurizoun,
Kai ena nekrokrevvato oi astrapes fwtizoun
Afhte tous| me arethn kai pistin agapousan,
Ston tafo kan enw8hkan, an oxi oso zousan!

Einai mia wraia periplanhsh, sxedon mia drapeteush -

        mas - mia e3aisia ais8hsh

        skoteino xrhmatokivwtio

anakalupteis pws auto to xrhmatokivwtio

        xartonomismata

Kai meneis monos m' olo sou ton plouto podopathmeno,

Martures gia ta la8h sou den eixes. Monos marturas

I

Auta ta dentra de voleuontai me ligotero ourano,
autes oi petres de voleuontai katou ap' ta 3ena vhmata,
auta ta proswpa de voleuontai para mono ston hlio,
autes oi kardies de voleuontai para mono sto dikio.

Etouto to topio einai sklhro san th siwph,
sfiggei ston korfo tou ta purwmena tou li8aria,
sfiggei sto fws tis orfanes elies tou kai t' ampelia tou,
sfiggei ta dontia. Den uparxei nero. Monaxa fws.
O dromos xanetai sto fws ki o iskios ths mantras einai sidero.
Marmarwsan ta dentra, ta potamia k' oi fwnes mes ston asve-
      sth tou hliou.
H riza skontaftei sto marmaro. Ta skonismena skoina.
To moulari ki o vraxos. Laxaniazoun. Den uparxei nero.
Oloi diyane. Xronia twra. Oloi masane mia mpoukia ourano
      panou ap' thn pikra tous.
Ta matia tous einai kokkina ap' thn agrupnia,
mia va8eia xarakia sfhnwmenh anamesa sta frudia tous
san ena kuparissi anamesa se duo vouna to liogerma.

To xeri tous einai kollhmeno sto ntoufeki
to ntoufeki einai sunexeia tou xeriou tous
to xeri tous einai sunexeia ths yuxhs tous -
exoun sta xeilia tous apanou to 8umo
k' exoune ton kahmo va8ia-va8ia sta matia tous
san ena asteri se mia gouva alati.

Otan sfiggoun to xeri, o hlios einai vevaios gia ton kosmo
otan xamogelane, ena mikro xelidoni feugei mes ap' t' agria ge-
      neia tous
otan koimountai, dwdeka astra peftoun ap' tis adeies tsepes tous
otan skotwnontai, h zwh travaei thn anhfora me shmaies kai
      me tampourla.

Tosa xronia oloi peinane, oloi diyane, oloi skotwnontai
poliorkhmenoi apo steria kai 8alassa,
efage h kaya ta xwrafia tous k' h armura potise ta spitia tous
o ageras erri3e tis portes tous kai tis liges pasxalies ths plateias
apo tis trupes tou panwforiou tous mpainovgainei o 8anatos
h glwssa tous einai stufh san to kuparissomhlo
pe8anan ta skulia tous tuligmena ston iskio tous
h vroxh xtupaei sta kokkala tous.

Panou sta karaoulia petrwmenoi kapnizoun th svounia kai th 
      nuxta
viglizontas to maniasmeno pelago opou voulia3e 
to spasmeno katarti tou feggariou.

To ywmi sw8hke, ta volia sw8hkan,
gemizoun twra ta kanonia tous mono me thn kardia tous.

Tosa xronia poliorkhmenoi apo steria kai 8alassa
oloi peinane, oloi skotwnontai kai kanenas den pe8ane -
panou sta karaoulia lampoune ta matia tous,
mia megalh shmaia, mia megalh fwtia katakokkinh
kai ka8e augh xiliades peristeria feugoun ap' ta xeria tous
gia tis tesseris portes tou orizonta.


II

Ka8e pou vradiazei me to 8umari tsourouflismeno ston korfo
      ths petras
einai mia stagona nero pou skavei apo palia th siwph ws to
      medouli
einai mia kampana kremasmenh sto gero-platano pou fwnazei
      ta xronia.

Spi8es lagokoimountai sth xovolh ths erhmias
k' oi steges sullogiountai to malamatenio xnoudi sto panw xeili
      tou Alwnarh
- kitrino xnoudi san th founta tou kalampokiou kapnismeno
      ap' ton kahmo ths dushs.

H Panagia plagiazei stis murties me th fardeia ths fousta
      lekiasmenh ap' ta stafulia.
Sto dromo klaiei ena paidi kai tou apokrinetai ap' ton kampo
      h provatina pouxei xasei ta paidia ths.

Iskios sth vrush. Pagwmeno to vareli.
H korh tou petalwth me mouskemena podia.
Apanou sto trapezi to ywmi k' h elia,
mes sthn klhmataria o luxnos tou aposperith
kai kei yhla, gurizontas sth souvla tou, euwdaei o gala3ias 
kameno 3ugki, skordo kai piperi.

A, ti mprisimi asteri akoma 8a xreiastei
gia na kenthsoun oi peukovelones sthn kayalismenh mantra tou
      kalokairiou "ki auto 8a perasei"
poso 8a stiyei akoma h mana thn kardia ths panou ap' ta efta
      sfagmena pallhkaria ths
wspou na vre'i to fws to dromo tou sthn anhfora ths yuxhs ths.

Touto to kokkalo pou vgainei apo th ghs
metraei orgia-orgia th ghs kai tis kordes tou lagoutou
kai to lagouto aposperis me to violi ws to xarama
kahmo-kahmo to len sta duosmarinia kai stous peukous
kai ntintinizoun sta karavia ta skoinia san kordes
ki o nauths pinei pikro8alassa sthn koupa tou Odussea.

A, poios 8a fra3ei totes th mpasia kai poio spa8i 8a koyei
      to kouragio
kai poio kleidi 8a sou kleidwsei thn kardia pou me ta duo 8uro-
      fulla ths diaplata
koitaei tou 8eou t' astroperixuta pervolia;

wra megalh san ta Savvatovrada tou Mah sth nautikh taverna
nuxta megalh san tayi stou ganwtzh ton toixo
megalo to tragoudi san ywmi stou sfouggara to deipno.
Kai na pou rovolaei ta troxala to krhtiko feggari
gkap, gkap, me eikosi arades prokadoura sta stivalia tou,
kai natoi autoi pou anevokatevainoune th skala tou Anapliou
gemizontas thn pipa tous xontrokommena fulla apo skotadi,
me to moustaki tous 8umari roumeliwtiko paspalismeno asteri
kai me to donti tous peukorriza stou Aigaiou to vraxo kai to 
      alati.
Mphkan sta sidera kai sth fwtia, kouventiasan me ta li8aria,
kerasane raki to 8anato sto kaukalo tou pappoulh tous,
st' Alwnia ta idia antamwsan to Digenh kai strw8hkan sto 
      deipno
kovontas ton kahmo sta duo etsi pou kovane sto gonato to kri-
      8arenio tous karveli.

Ela kura me t' armura matoklada, me flwrokapnismeno xeri
apo thn egnoia tou ftwxou ki ap' ta polla ta xronia -
h agaph se permenei mes sta skoina,
mes sth sphlia tou o glaros sou kremaei to mauro konisma sou
ki o pikramenos axinios sou aspazetai to nuxi tou podiou sou.
Mesa sth maurh rwga tou ampeliou koxlazei o moustos kata-
      kokkinos,
koxlazei to rodami ston kameno prino,
sto xwma h riza tou nekrou zhtaei nero gia na tina3ei elati
k' h mana katou ap' th rutida ths krataei gera maxairi.
Ela kura pou ta xrusa klwssas auga tou keraunou -
pote mia mera 8alassia 8a vgaleis to tsemperi kai 8a pareis
      pali t' armata
na se xtuphsei katakoutela magiatiko xalazi
na spasei roidi o hlios sthn alatzadenia sou podia
na ton moiraseis monh sou spuri-spuri sta dwdeka orfana sou,
na lamyei ologura o gialos ws lampei h koyh tou spa8iou kai 
      t' Apriliou to xioni
kai navgei sta xalikia o kavouras gia na liastei kai na stau-
      rwsei tis dagkanes tou.


III

Dw pera o ouranos de ligosteuei oute stigmh to ladi tou ma-
      tiou mas
dw pera o hlios pairnei panw tou to miso varos ths petras 
      pou shkwnoume panta sth raxh mas
spane ta keramidia dixws ax katou ap' to gona tou meshmeriou
oi an8rwpoi pan mprosta ap' ton iskio tous san ta delfinia
      mpros ap' ta skia8itika kaikia
ustera o iskios tous ginetai enas a itos pou vafei ta ftera tou
      sto liogerma
kai pio ustera kourniazei sto kefali tous kai sullogietai t' astra
otan autoi plagiazoune sto liakwto me th maurh stafida.

Dw pera h ka8e porta exei pelekhmeno ena onoma kapou apo 
      treis xiliades tosa xronia
ka8e li8ari exei zwgrafismenon enan agio m' agria matia kai
      mallia skoinenia
ka8e antras exei sto zervi tou xeri xaragmenh velonia th ve-
      lonia mia kokkinh gorgona
ka8e kopela exei mia fouxta alatismeno fws katou ap' th 
      fousta ths
kai ta paidia exoun pente-e3i stauroulakia pikra panou sthn
      kardia tous
san ta xnaria ap' to vhma twn glarwn sthn ammoudia to apogeuma.

De xreiazetai na 8umh8eis. To 3eroume.
Ola ta monopatia vgazoune sta yhlalwnia. O ageras einai
      ayus kei panou.

'Otan 3eftaei apomakra h minwikh toixografia ths dushs
kai svhnei h purka ia ston axerwna ths akrogialias
anhforizoun ws edw oi gries ap' ta skammena sto vraxo skalo-
      patia
ka8ountai sth Megalh Petra gne8ontas me ta matia th 8alassa
ka8ountai kai metran t' asteria ws na metrane ta progonika
      ashmenia tous koutalophrouna
ki arga kathforane na taisoune ta eggonia tous me to mesolog-
      gitiko mparouti.

Nai, alh8eia, o Elkomenos exei duo xeria toso luphmena mesa 
      sth 8hleia tous
omws to frudi tou saleuei san to vraxo pou olo paei na 3e-
      kollhsei panou ap' to pikro tou mati.
Apo va8ia anevainei auto to kuma pou den 3erei parakalia
apo yhla kulaei autos o ageras me retsini fleva kai plemoni
      alisfakia.

Ax, 8a fush3ei mia na parei svarna tis portokalies ths 8u-
      mhshs
Ax, 8a fush3ei duo na vgalei spi8a h siderenia petra san
      kayouli
Ax, 8a fush3ei treis kai 8a trellanei ta elatodasa sth Lia-
      koura
8a dwsei mia me th gro8ia tou na tina3ei thn turagnia ston
      agera
kai 8a travh3ei ths arkoudas nuxtas to xalka na mas xoreyei
      tsamiko katamesis sthn tapia
kai ntefi to feggari 8a xtupaei pou na gemisoun ta nhsiwtika
      mpalkonia
agouro3upnhmeno paidoloi kai souliwtisses manades.

Enas mantatoforos ftanei ap' th Megalh Lagkadia ka8e
      prwino
sto proswpo tou lampei o idrwmenos hlios
katou apo th maskalh tou kratei sfixta th rwmiosunh
opws krataei o ergaths thn tragiaska tou mesa sthn ekklhsia.
Hr8e h wra, leei. Namaste etoimoi.
Ka8e wra einai h dikia mas wra.


IV

Travh3an oloisia sthn augh me thn akatade3ia tou an8rwpou
      pou peinaei,
mesa st' asaleuta matia tous eixe ph3ei ena astro
ston wmo tous kouvalagan to lavwmeno kalokairi.

Apo dw perase o stratos me ta flampoura katasarka
me to peisma dagkwmeno sta dontia tous san agouro gkortsi
me ton ammo tou feggariou mes stis arvules tous
kai me thn karvounoskonh ths nuxtas kollhmenh mesa sta rou-
      8ounia kai st' autia tous.

Dentro to dentro, petra-petra perasan ton kosmo,
m' agka8ia proskefali perasan ton upno.
Fernan th zwh sta duo stegna tous xeria san potami.

Se ka8e vhma kerdizan mia orgia ourano - gia na ton dwsoun.
Panou sta karaoulia petrwnan san ta kayaliasmena dentra,
ki otan xoreuan sthn plateia,
mesa sta spitia treman ta tavania kai koudounizan ta gualika
      sta rafia.

A, ti tragoudi tranta3e ta korfovounia -
anamesa sta gonata tous kratagan to skouteli tou feggariou
      kai deipnousan,
kai spagan to ax mesa sta fullokardia tous
sa naspagan mia yeira anamesa sta duo xontra tous nuxia.

Poios 8a sou ferei twra to zesto karveli mes sth nuxta na
      taiseis ta oneira;
Poios 8a sta8ei ston iskio ths elias parea me to tzitziki mh
      swpasei to tzitziki,
twra pou asvesths tou meshmeriou vafei th mantra ologura
      tou orizonta
svhnontas ta megala antrikia onomata tous;

To xwma touto pou moskovolouse ta xaramata
to xwma pou eitane diko tous kai diko mas - aima tous - pws
      murize to xwma -
kai twra pws kleidwsane thn porta tous t' ampelia mas
pws ligneye to fws stis steges kai sta dentra
poios na to pei pws vriskontai oi misoi katou ap' to xwma 
k' oi alloi misoi sta sidera;

Me tosa fulla na sou gnefei o hlios kalhmera
me tosa flampoura na lampei o ouranos
kai toutoi mes sta sidera kai keinoi mes sto xwma.

Swpa, opou nanai 8a shmanoun oi kampanes.
Auto to xwma einai diko tous kai diko mas.
Katou ap' to xwma, mes sta staurwmena xeria tous
kratane ths kampanas to skoini - permenoune thn wra, den
      koimountai,
permenoun na shmanoun thn anastash. Touto to xwma
einai diko tous kai diko mas - de mporei kaneis na mas to parei.


V

Katsane katou ap' tis elies to apomeshmero
koskinizontas to staxti fws me ta xontra tous daxtula
vgalane tis mpalaskes tous kai logariazan posos moxtos xwrese
      sto monopati ths nuxtas
posh pikra ston kompo ths agriomoloxas
poso kouragio mes sta matia tou 3upolutou paidiou pou kratae
      th shmaia.

Eixe apomeinei parwra ston kampo to sterno xelidoni
zugiazotan ston aera sa mia maurh lourida sto maniki tou f8i-
      nopwrou.
Tipot' allo den emene. Monaxa kapnizan akoma ta kamena spitia.
Oi alloi mas afhsan apo kairo katou ap' tis petres
me to skismeno tous poukamiso kai me ton orko tous grammeno
      sthn pesmenh porta.
Den eklaye kaneis. Den eixame kairo. Mono pou h sigalia me-
      galwne polu
k' eitan to fws sugurismeno katou sto gialo san to noikokurio
      ths skotwmenhs.

Ti 8a ginoun twra otan 8ar8ei h vroxh mes sto xwma me ta
      sapia platanofulla
ti 8a ginoun otan o hlios stegnwsei sto xrami ths sugnefias
      sa spasmenos korios sto xwriatiko krevvati
otan sta8ei sthn kaminada tou apovradou mpalsamwmeno to
      leleki tou xioniou;
Pixnoune alati oi gries manades sth fwtia, rixnoune xwma sta 
      mallia tous
3errizwsan t' ampelia ths Monovasias mh kai glukanei maurh
      rwga twn extrwn to stoma,
valan s' ena sakkouli twn pappoudwn tous ta kokkala mazi me
      ta maxairophrouna
kai trigurnane e3w ap' ta teixh ths patridas tous yaxnontas 
      topo na rizwsoune sth nuxta.

8anai duskolo twra na vroume mia glwssa pio ths kerasias,
      ligotero dunath, ligotero petrinh -
ta xeria ekeina pou apomeinan sta xwrafia h apanou sta vouna
      h katou ap' th 8alassa, den 3exnane -
8anai duskolo na 3exasoume ta xeria tous
8anai duskolo ta xeria pouvgalan kalous sth skandalh na rw-
      thsoun mia margarita
na poun euxaristw panou sto gonato tous, panou sto vivlio h
      mes sto mpousto ths astrofeggias.
8a xreiastei kairos. Kai prepei na milhsoume. wspou na vroun
      to ywmi kai to dikio tous.

Duo koupia karfwmena ston ammo ta xaramata me th four-
      touna. Pounai h varka;
Ena aletri mphgmeno sto xwma, ki o ageras na fusaei. Kameno
      to xwma. Pounai o zeugolaths;
Staxth h elia, t' ampeli kai to spiti.
Bradia spaggorammenh me t' asteria ths mes sto tsourapi.
Dafnh 3erh kai riganh sto mesontoulapo tou toixou. Den t'
      aggi3e h fwtia.
Kapnismeno tsoukali sto tzaki - kai na koxlazei mono to nero
      sto kleidwmeno spiti. Den proftasan na fane.

Apanw sto kameno tous portofullo oi fleves tou dasous - tre-
      xei to aima mes stis fleves.
Kai na to vhma gnwrimo. Poios einai;
Gnwrimo vhma me tis prokes ston anhforo.
To sursimo ths rizas mes sthn petra. Kapoios erxetai.
To sun8hma, to parasun8hma. Adelfos. Kalhspera.
8a vrei loipon to fws ta dentra tou, 8a vrei mia mera kai to 
      dentro ton karpo tou.
Tou skotwmenou to pagouri exei nero kai fws akoma.
Kalhspera, aderfe mou. To 3ereis. Kalhspera.

Sthn 3ulinh paragka ths poulaei mpaxarika kai ntemisedes h
      gria dush.
Kaneis den agorazei. Travh3an yhla.
Duskolo pia na xamhlwsoun.
Duskolo kai na poun to mpoi tous.

Mesa st' alwni opou deipnhsan mia nuxtia ta pallhkaria
menoune ta liokoukoutsa kai to aima to 3ero tou feggariou
ki o dekapentasullavos ap' t' armata tous.
Thn allh mera ta spourgitia fagane ta yixoula ths kouramanas
      tous,
ta paidia ftia3ane paixnidia me ta spirta tous pou anayan ta
      tsigara tous kai t' agka8ia twn astrwn.

K' h petra opou ka8hsan katou ap' tis elies to apomeshmero
      antikru sth 8alassa
aurio 8a ginei asvesths sto kamini
me8aurio 8' asvestwsoume ta spitia mas kai to pezouli ths 
      Agia-Swthras
antime8aurio 8a futeyoume to sporo ekei pou apokoimh8hkan
k' ena mpoumpouki ths rodias 8a skasei prwto gelio tou mwrou
      ston korfo ths liakadas.
K' ustera pia 8a katsoume sthn petra na diavasoume olh thn 
      kardia tous
sa na diavazoume prwth fora thn istoria tou kosmou.


VI

Etsi me ton hlio katasth8a sto pelago pou asvestwnei thn
      antikrunh plagia ths meras
logariazetai dipla kai tridipla to mantalwma kai to vasano ths 
      diyas
logariazetai ap' thn arxh h palia lavwmatia
k' h kardia 3eroyhnetai sthn kaya san ta vatikiwtika kremmu-
      dia mpros stis portes.

Oso pane ta xeria tous moiazoune piotero to xwma
oso pane ta matia tous moiazoune piotero ton ourano.

Adeiase to kioupi me to ladi. Ligh mourga ston pato. Ki o 
      yofios pontikos.
Adeiase to kouragio ths manas mazi me to phlino kanati kai
      th sterna.
Stufizoun ta oula ths ermias ap' to mparouti.

Pou ladi twra pia gia to kanthli ths Agia-Barvaras
pou duosmos pia na livanisei to malamatenio konisma tou deilinou
pou mia mpoukia ywmi gia th vradia-zhtiana na sou pai3ei thn 
      astromantinada ths sth lura.

Sto panou kastro tou nhsiou stoixeiwsan oi fragkosukies kai
      ta sperdouklia.
To xwma anaskammeno apo to kanonidi kai tous tafous.
To gkremismeno Dioikhthrio mpalwmeno me ourano. Den exei pia
      ka8olou topo
gia allous nekrous. Den exei topo h luph na sta8ei na ple3ei 
      ta mallia ths.

Spitia kamena pou agnanteuoun me vgalmena matia to marmarw-
      meno pelago
k' oi sfaires sfhnwmenes sta teixia
san ta maxairia sta paidia tou Agiou pou ton desane sto ku-
      parissi.

Olh th mera oi skotwmenoi liazontai anaskela ston hlio.
Kai mono sa vradiazei oi stratiwtes sernontai me thn koilia
      stis kapnismenes petres
yaxnoun me ta rou8ounia ton agera e3w ap' to 8anato
yaxnoune ta papoutsia tou feggariou masoulwntas ena kommati
      mentzesola
xtupan me th gro8ia to vraxo mhpws tre3ei o kompos tou nerou
ma ap' thn allh meria o toixos einai koufios
kai 3anakoun to xtuphma me tous pollous gurous pou kanei h
      ovida peftontas sth 8alassa
ki akoun akoma mia fora to skou3imo twn lavwmenwn mpros
      sthn pulh.
Pou na travh3eis; Se fwnazei o aderfos sou.

Xtismenh h nuxta ologura ap' tous iskious 3enwn karaviwn.
Kleismenoi oi dromoi ap' ta ntouvaria. 
Mono gia ta yhla einai akoma dromos.
Ki autoi mountzwnoun ta karavia kai dagkwnoune th glwssa tous
n' akousoune ton pono tous pou den egine kokkalo.

Apanw sta mentenia oi skotwmenoi kapetanioi or8oi frouroun
      to kastro.
Katou ap' ta rouxa tous luwnoun ta kreata tous. Ei, aderfi,
      den apostases;
Mpoumpoukiase to voli mesa sthn kardia sou
pente zoumpoulia 3emutisan sth maskalh tou 3erovraxou,
anasa-anasa h moskovolia leei to paramu8i - de 8umasai;
dontia-dontia h lavwmatia sou leei th zwh,
to xamomhli futrwmeno mes sth ligda tou nuxiou sou sto me-
      galo daxtulo tou podariou
sou leei thn omorfia tou kosmou.

Pianeis to xeri. Einai diko sou. Notismeno ap' thn armura.
Dikia sou h 8alassa. San 3errizwneis trixa ap' to kefali ths
      siwphs
stazei pikro to gala ths sukias. Opou kai nasai o ouranos se
      vlepei.
Strivei sta daxtula tou o aposperiths thn yuxh sou san tsigaro
etsi nan th foumareis thn yuxh sou anaskela
vrexontas to zervi sou xeri mes sthn 3asteria
kai sto de3i sou kollhmeno to ntoufeki-arravwniastikia sou
na 8umh8eis pws o ouranos pote tou de se 3exase
otan 8a vgazeis ap' th mesa tseph to palio tou gramma
kai 3ediplwnontas me daxtula kamena to feggari 8a diavazeis
      leventia kai do3a.

ustera 8' aneveis sto yhlo karaouli tou nhsiou sou
kai vazontas kayouli to astro 8a travh3eis mia ston aera
panou apo ta teixia kai ta katartia
panou apo ta vouna pou skuvoun sa fantaroi plhgwmenoi
etsi mono kai mono na xougia3eis ta stoixeia kai na trupwsoun
      sthn kouverta tou iskiou -
8a ri3eis mian isa ston korfo t' ouranou na vreis to galano 
      shmadi
sampws na vriskeis panou ap' to poukamiso th rwga ths gu-
      naikas pou aurio 8a vuzainei to paidi sou
sampws na vriskeis uster' apo xronia to xerouli ths e3wportas 
      tou patrikou spitiou sou.


VII

To spiti, o dromos, h fragkosukia, ta floudia tou hliou sthn 
      aulh pou ta tsimpologan oi kottes.
Ta 3eroume, mas 3eroune. Dw xamou anamesa sta vata
exei h dentrogalia parathmeno to kitrino poukamiso ths.
Dw xamou einai h kaluva tou mermhgkiou ki o purgos ths sfh-
      gkas me tis polles polemistres,
sthn idia elia to tsofli tou persinou tzitzika k' h fwnh tou
      feteinou tzitzika,
sta skoina o iskios sou pou se pairnei apo pisw sa skuli ami-
      lhto, polu vasanismeno,
pisto skuli - ta meshmeria ka8etai dipla sto xwmatenion upno
      sou murizontas tis pikrodafnes
ta vradia koulouriazetai sta podia sou koitazontas ena astro.

Einai mia sigalia apo axladia pou megalwnoune sta skelia tou
      kalokairiou
mia nusta apo nero pou xazeuei stis rizes ths xaroupias -
h anoi3h exei tria orfana koimismena sthn podia ths 
enan a ito misope8ameno sta matia ths
kai kei yhla pisw apo to peukodaso
stegnwnei to 3wkklhsi tou Ah-Gianniou tou Nhsteuth
san asprh koutsoulia tou spourgitiou s' ena platu fullo mou-
      rias pou thn 3erainei h kaya.

Etoutos o tsopanos tuligmenos thn provia tou
exei se ka8e trixa tou kormiou ena stegno potami
exei ena dasos velanidies se ka8e trupa ths flogeras tou
kai to ravdi tou exei tous idious rozous me to koupi pou prw-
      toxtuphse to galazio tou Ellhspontou.

De xreiazetai na 8umh8eis. H fleva tou platanou
exei to aima sou. Kai to sperdoukli tou nhsiou k' h kaparh.
To amilhto phgadi anevazei sto katameshmero
mia stroggulh fwnh apo mauro guali ki apo aspro anemo
stroggulh san ta palia pi8aria - h idia panarxaih fwnh.
Ka8e nuxta to feggari anapodogurizei tous skotwmenous
yaxnei ta proswpa tous me pagwmena daxtula na vrei to gio tou
ap' thn koyia tou sagoniou ki ap' ta petrina frudia,
yaxnei tis tsepes tous. Panta kati 8a vrei. Kati vriskoume.
Ena kleidi, ena gramma, ena roloi stamathmeno stis efta. Kour-
      ntizoume pali to roloi. Perpatane oi wres.

Otan me8aurio luwsoune ta rouxa tous kai meinoune gumnoi ana-
      mesa sta stratiwtika koumpia tous
etsi pou menoun ta kommatia t' ouranou anamesa apo ta kalo-
      kairiatika astra
tote mporei na vroume t' onoma tous kai mporei na to fwna-
      3oume: agapw.
Tote. Ma pali auta ta pragmata einai ligaki san polu makrina.
Einai ligaki san polu kontina, san otan pianeis sto skotadi ena
      xeri kai les kalhspera

O xronos den me 8elei pia. Paei, twra, polus kairos pou vlepw monaxa thn plath tou.
     Krufes arrwsties me diekdikoun, ma sunexizw, opws mporw, etouth th makra 8hteia.
     Trianta e3i xronia perasan kiolas apo th mera ekeinh pou eida gia prwth kai teleutaia fora ton pappou mou dixws o idios na me vlepei. Htan mia mera me vroxh kai kathforize sth mustikh plagia twn Filan8rwphnwn.
     Apo wres sfhnwmenos sto sanidenio teleutaio paltoudaki tou kai me to proswpo tou kitrino kai akampto, les ki htan skalismeno se sklhro turi, kumatize panw ap' ta xorta ths plagias kai tis vregmenes petres, ka8ws ekeinoi pou ton shkwnan den etuxe na exoune to idio uyos. Mono kati mavia louloudia tremane dipla sta kitrina -ap' ton polu kapno- moustakia, les kai dunameis skoteines eixan val8ei, thn wra ekeinh, na tou kanoun plaka.
     Apo th mera auth kai ustera, to dromo tou pappou mou akolou8hsan -dixws seira proteraiothtas- kai oi upoloipoi mou suggeneis pou vriskontan -sthn alusida pou mas enwne- mprost' apo mena.

Ka8e fora pou paw ston aderfo mou, thn pataw. To vlemma mou karfwnetai se keinh thn palia fwtografia pou exei kremasmenh panw ap' ton kanape. Koitazw mesa ekei, loipon, ta hliotropia tou patrikou mas khpou, pou, san uperoxa fwtistika, skuvane apo panw mas rixnontas fws aspromauro stou kefaliou mas th fountitsa kai menw, panta, me thn ais8hsh pws den perasan oute duo lepta ap' th stigmh ekeinh: apo th mera, dhladh, auth ths anoi3hs pou, krathmenoi ap' to xeri, stekame mprosta sto fwtografiko fako pou mas apa8anatise -saranta pente xronia prin- mesa s' auto ton khpo.
 
As einai. Agorasa, loipon, ap' to periptero to deutero paketo ths hmeras kai t' anoi3a phgainontas pros th meria pou eix' afhsei t' autokinhto.
     Enas aeras kruos fusage ta mizera dentrakia pou, sfhnwmena sto tsimento, emoiazan san na fulagane skopia e3w ap' to kleisto kai fwtismeno, m' ena fws prasinwpo, kreopwleio ths apenanti pleuras.
     Xwris na 3erw to giati, amesws perasa apenanti kai sta8hka mprosta stis pageres vitrines me ta kreata, anavontas tsigaro.
     Pisw ap' to tzami -sthn ka8eth kolona autou tou magaziou- enas ka8refths m' edeixne na me koitw etsi opws hmoun akrivws, auth thn wra: enas antras pou 'xei perasei apo panw tou oloklhrh h zwh, penhnta pente xronwn, monos tou ki anaudos sthn erhmia auths ths sunoikias, me to pikro tsigaro tou na kremetai sthn akrh twn xeiliwn, ki olo na stelnei pros to nuxtwmeno ourano ekeino ton lepto kapno, les kai sunexize thn proseuxh pou eix' afhsei ateleiwth, prin apo xronia, o pappous tou s' allo meros.
     Blepontas thn eikona auth, suneidhtopoihsa akariaia, pws eixa meinei monos pia, dixws kanenan suggenh mou pros ta pisw. H alusida pou me enwne m' autous eixe kopei apo kairo ki egw stekomoun twra aporhmenos ki anaudos sthn akrh auths ths klimakas -pou odhgei me tropo ma8hmatiko pros thn anupar3ia- afou h zwh to 8elhse na eimai pia o megaluteros se hlikia ap' olous mou tous suggeneis pou zoun s' authn edw th xwra, parolo pou, apo kairo pio prin, 8a eprepe na to 'xa upopteu8ei pws 8a sunevaine ki auto, ka8ws o 8eios mou o Xarilaos mou thlefwnage -to kalokairi pou mas perase- sunexeia kai mou zhtouse an htan dunaton na epanalavoume, gia mia fora akomh, ekeinh thn palia voltitsa stous agrous e3w ap' th gene8lia polh.
     E keinh thn anemelh podhlatada tou '56 mou zhtage na epanalavoume -phgainontas arga kai kouventiazontas oi duo mas- mexri th vrush tou Pasa, asxeta an twra pia o topos ekei gurw exei alla3ei entelws afou xtisthkan oi agroi kai mplok, oloklhra, katoikiwn or8w8hkan s' auto to meros, mexri yhla, sthn tafro ekeinh me ta xamomhlia, opou palia htan to sunoro gia tous fumatikous: ekeinous tous fumatikous pou zousane, suxna, kleismenoi pisw ap' ta kagkela tou sanatoriou, ma katevainane krufa mexri thn tafro auth -idiws tis giortes ths anoi3hs- kai, me ta matia flogismena ap' ton pureto, koitazane me po8o ki agapousan noera oles ekeines tis apokrhmnes gunaikes, pou, kapote, agaphsame ki emeis apelpismena.
 
An den to eixa apo tote upopteu8ei 8a eprepe, toulaxiston, na to'xa katalavei pia, duo mhnes akrivws argotera, otan ekeinh h gunaika sto 8hseio 8a evlepe, sta kataka8ia tou kafe pou molis eixa piei, to 8anato tou 8eiou mou treis wres prin me parei sto thlefwno o 3aderfos mou o Basilhs gia na mou pei, oti st' alh8eia twra pia, o 8eios mou o Xarilaos, eixe duo wres pou 'xe fugei apo touth th zwh oristika, kai ekane podhlatada monos tou ston ourano.
 
Apenanti mou, sto komo, dipla ston mauro elefanta, pou phra ap' to Monasthraki, ena roloi tou mesopolemou xwneuei, hxhrotata, ta deuterolepta pou -me epifwnhmata, metallika, monotona- peftoun nekra, to ena pisw ap' t' allo, mesa ekei, sth siderenia tou koilia, upen8umizontas mou, me ton tropo tous, pws tipote den stamata. O 8anatos ergazetai akatapausta opws, e3allou, ki h zwh, afou, thn idia wra sto mpalkoni mou vlepw ta prwta fulla ths klhmatarias pou 3ephdhsan hdh trufera kai kataprasina -stis akres tou stegnou ths tou kormou, uphretwntas sta tufla, gia mia fora akomh, ths fushs to panarxaio kai skoteino ka8hkon.
 
Kai na pou hr8e pali h anoi3h| 8a 'r8ei kai to kalokairaki.
     To niw8w. Kapoios mesa mou arxise na sfurizei sigana ekeino ton palio skopo pou h3ere ki h mana mou. 

Mesa s' auta ta xronia pou perasane, para pollous an8rwpous etuxe na gnwrisw. Pollous 8umamai akomh, ma akomh pio pollous exw 3exasei pia. Aeras dunatos mas exei parasurei kai mas skorpise. Par' ol' auta, uparxoun filoi mou kaloi s' authn edw thn polh, ma oi pio polloi menoun makria ki olo pio spania tous vlepw. Ftia3ane oikogeneies ki alla3ane ru8mo zwhs. Kapoioi ap' autous menoun sta voreia proastia kai alloi, pali, katoikoun katw, sth notioanatolikh pleura pros th meria ths 8alassas: se polukatoikies axares h kai se spitia idiokthta, me khpous austhrous -olo mpeton kai kokkinoxwma me mizera dentrakia kai stenous diadromous kai me kati skulous-fulakes pou me gaugizoun agria san na 'mai klefths ka8e fora pou katafernw, mes sth nuxta na ftasw ws ekei gia na tous dw.
     Pantws, oi apostaseis kai h zwh pou kanoume ka8olou den mas voh8a na eidw8oume, gi' auto, kai toutes oi filies exoun e3elix8ei pia se filies thlefwnikes.
     Pote mou den ta phgaina kala me to thlefwno, ma akomh pio polu variemai ki autes tis axares kai makrines diadromes s' auth thn polh-xwra, opou eimai anagkasmenos pia na zw kai na pernaw th mish mou zwh, me deuterh taxuthta, stous dromous ths parea me tous allous pou olo me koitoun, pisw ap' ta tzamia tou autokinhtou tous, me vlemma agrio kai apeilhtiko les ki eim' egw, proswpika, o kurios upeu8unos gi' auto to xali h alles fores pali, mou apeu8unoun feugalea vlemmata sunenoxhs kai katanohshs, vlepontas, sto proswpo mou, akomh enan as8enh pou exei prosvlh8ei ap' thn aniath arrwstia auths ths polhs.
     Etsi, loipon, siga-siga, me touta kai me t' alla ta katafera, entelei, na ginw ki egw tupos ekdromikos s' auth thn hlikia: enas tupos sportif tou kleistou xwrou exw katanthsei me liga logia, mias kai oi diadromes mou, ton teleutaio kairo, exoun perioristei sxedon sto xwro mono twn dwmatiwn tou spitiou, alla oi ekdromes mou pia exoun pollaplasiastei kai exoun ginei aperioristou xronou.
     Me trigurizoune xiliades antikeimena kai to megalo mou dwmatio exei metatrapei s' ena topio pou allazei sunexws, analoga me th dia8esh pou me katexei. Allazw klimaka, optikh ki olh th mera analwnomai se eswterikes diadromes: diadromes se topous mustikous pou arxizoun ap' ton skouro kampo tou anatolitikou paniou, me to opoio einai skepasmeno to ntivani, mexri ta roz papakia tou trapezomantilou, pou akolou8oun se taktikes grammes -to ena pisw ap' t' allo- kai diasxizoun ru8mika olo to mhkos tou megalou trapeziou, stenazontas katw ap' to varos twn dekadwn moluviwn, ths suskeuhs to thlefwnou, ths koupas me ta kataka8ia tou kafe, twn gualinwn staxtodoxeiwn pou orizoun tis perioxes kapnismatos -analoga me thn wra ths meras kai th dia8esh- ka8ws kai thn akatasxeth maurh vroxoula twn le3ewn pou trexei panw sta skorpia fulla tou xartiou kai tous kleinei th 8ea pros ta panw.
 
Na, twra da, exw edw mprosta mou ena ap' auta ta magika ta antikeimena pou katakluzoun to trapezi. E inai ena mikro sideriko pou lampei mes sth nuxta kai moiazei me e3wtiko pouli: me almpatros metalliko, moiazei, pou omws den peta, gia ta 8erma nera den feugei| oute voltitses kovei, sthrigmeno sta yhloligna tou podia, mesa se keines tis gnwstes seires ntokumanter, katw stis limnes tou alatiou, ekei sth maurh hpeiro me thn avastaxth th zesth, para monaxa -gia xatiri mou- vu8izetai, suxna, sto phgadi ths 3ulinhs mou pipas kai me to rugxos tou skalizei tis pleures.
     Kommatia maura axrhstou kapnou kovei drasthria apo tis akres kai olo 3unei ta toixwmata anoigontas dromo euruxwro gia ton meta3wto kapno pou 8a ton katevasei h fwtia mesa se keino to makru diadromo ki amesws ustera, me tis megales eispnoes 8a proxwrhsei sta va8ia kai 8a perasei, san phxtos staxtus aeras -anamesa se mia seira apo maurismena dontia- sta malaka kai roz toixwmata. 8a katevei, sth sunexeia, se keinh thn apotomh tsoulh8ra me to apeilhtiko sarkwdes zwo ths 8hlhs na kremetai apo panw tou -omoio me ta para3ena kai ahdiastika zwa twn tainiwn tou Sphlmpergk- kai san kolumvhths deinos 8a ftasei, grhgora, mexri tis kuyelides twn pneumonwn kai 8a xtuphsei sto vathra ths epistrofhs. 8a epistreyei etsi pia apo thn idia odo h 8a trupwsei ena meros tou sto diplano diadromo gia na perasei, amesws ustera, apo ta trixwta rou8ounia, eleu8erwnontas -estw kai stigmiaia- m' auto ton tropo, to varos mias yuxhs agxwmenhs, pou trizei xronia stis stoes tou akatanohtou pou thn krataei egkleisth, gia mia oloklhrh zwh, xwris pote na dinei kapoia lush.
     Saranta xronia perasan sxedon apo th mera pou katafera na mpw s' auth thn askoph diadikasia: ap' th stigmh ekeinh, dhladh, pou eniwsa -kapws aorista vevaia- oti travwntas pros ta sw8ika mou, me megales eispnoes, to mataio kapno, 8a katalavaina -oxi me to mualo ma me to swma- pws kata kapoio tropo a3ize ton kopo auth h kinhsh, afou me th dikh mou pia th 8elhsh kataferna n' apallagw, mesw ths ekpnohs, apo ena megalo meros ekeinou tou pikrou, phxtou aera pou 'xa katevasei mesa mou.
     Kanenas, vevaia, den m' anagkazei na to kanw auto, alla pragma para3eno, auth h diadikasia tou kapnismatos me fernei me tropo dramatiko polu konta s' auto pou 8a onomaza -kapws adokima vevaia- swmatikh proseggish sto mhxanismo tou akatanohtou.
     8umamai twra, san na 'tan xtes, thn aparxh| thn prwth mera, dhladh, auths ths askophs kai makras 8hteias.
     Htan ena prwino tou Marth me liakada. Phgaina tote, sthn trith ta3h ths E mporikhs kai eixa, hdh, duo-treis mhnes pou den forousa pia sunexeia ekeino to kapelo me tous ari8mous kai to ravdi to Kerdwou E rmh panw sthn prasinh lwrida me thn tsoxa. Tis pio polles fores to diplwna sta duo kai to 'xwna sthn tseph ki htan auto, as poume, kapoiou eidous tsaxpinia alla kai pra3h antistashs, tautoxrona, pros to katesthmeno.
     Mazi me allous treis summa8htes mou, th mera ekeinh, phga sto periptero tou platanou opou kai agorasame -me akra mustikothta- mish ntouzina xuma tsigara, ap' thn kouta, o ka8enas ki anti na pame, opws eprepe, sto ma8hma twn logistikwn, kateu8un8hkame, oloi mazi, pros to ghpedo -pou vriskotan sthn idia geitonia me to sxoleio- opou met' apo ligo, piasame to xamhlo mantrotoixo ths voreinhs pleuras, ekeinhs ths pleuras pou evlepe pros th meria ths limnhs kai to vraxna tou graniteniou ths vounou pou 3ekinouse ap' ta nera ki anevaine, san zwo pro istoriko, sta xilia tosa metra, kleinontas ton orizonta.
     Amesws, tote, dixws ka8usterhsh, arxise h giorth ekeinh pou etoimazame. San iereis mias mustikhs teletourgias -suspeirwmenoi kai apomakroi- me tis plates akoumpismenes ston xortariasmeno ton mantrotoixo, arxisame na katevazoume -sthn arxh, me distaktikes kai, sth sunexeia, me 8arralees roufh3ies- ekeino ton pikrotato kapno pou katevainontas sta sw8ika mas epnige sto vhxa, kanontas ta matia mas na plhmmurizoun apo dakrua: dakrua apognwshs, 8riamvou, alla kai xaras tautoxrona, afou ekeinh th stigmh pisteuame, akradanta, oti pernousame - mes' ap' to stadio auto ths muhshs- diamias sto xwro pia twn enhlikwn.

     Memias tote, oloi mazi -san sunwmotes kapoias etaireias Filikhs pou thn katedwsan- opws e3allou, to gnwrizame auto ki apo thn istoria -prodotes ek twn endon, san ailouroi skarfalwsame sto xamhlo mantrotoixo kai, egkataleipontas to ena trito tou teleutaiou mas tsigarou anekmetalleuto, phdh3ame suntonismenoi ayoga- pros to keno ths allhs pleuras xwris kan na eleg3oume to xwro apo katw.

Htan gumnos. Sthn polh ton petrovolousan. Ki efeuge, me to aima na stazei pisw tou. "8elei na deixnei anuperaspistos", elegan oi sofoi.

    san thn a8anasia twn poihtwn.

Xarismeno tou Giwrgou Katsimpalh


Den eitan h omorfoterh, ma eitan h pio tsakpina
    	k' eixe diko ths xou.
Gia dauth, legan, toustriyan, edw kai kana mhna,
    	tou Mpamph tou Lexou.

Gia dauth mparkaristhke kai tou Lakia t' agori,
    	pou to katapie h gh.
8a peis, autos den tw3ere to soi tou; gia thn korh
    	pws phe tou Mpenagh;

Pou auth, thn proskunhsane kefalia ki afentades,
    	afou ths phe gampros
ki o Mpikas ap' ta Salwna, pwxei ta spitia arades
    	stou Pepa, ligo mpros.

Ki o Nakos o kapnemporas, o gios tou Karantoula,
    	pwxei flouri m' oura,
ki apo kalos, de legetai| levenths me ta oula.
    	Kai 8aeitan mia kura.

Ki akoma thn pro3eneye-katakala to 3airw,
    	ma logos na mh vgei-
o tokisths o Topakas, alla ton eipan gero.
    	(Mas twlee h Xrusaugh.) 

Ma o Mpenaghs ton voleye, kai paei ki autos, me tropo,
    	ki as eixe t' aga8a,
kata pws mpaizogelage ka8e gampro ap' ton topo,
    	me t' aurio, me to 8a

Tetoia eitan h Aggelika, k' eitan monaxokorh
    	ki ws dekaefta xronw.
Ta eikosipente pathsa pou leipw ap' to Braxwri,
    	ma den th lhsmonw.

Giati me tous anupantrous, pouxan kairo gia gamo,
    	eitan k' oi pio mikroi.
T' amoustaka kai t' agoura, pou agapes 3eran, ammo,
    	ki apo kenteri, gri.

Mia kai den to 3eshkwnan oi topoi mas averta
    	o3w na vgainei h nia,
dos tou ki apo thn porta ths mprosta ta sourta-ferta|
    	sto podi h geitonia.

Kai gia na mhn tous pairnoune kai murwdia oi geitonoi,
    	pou olo katalaloun,
oi mualwmenoi fulagan to ntoro, sa nuxtwnei,
    	na mhn ton ntilaloun.

Ka8enas paei gia logou tou, ki wstoso pan antama.
    	K' oi agaphtikoi
suntrofika apofasizan gia na thn kleyoun, ama
    	th vriskan volikh.

Ma, san th vlepan, legane, ta spitia kai gurizan,
    	ki an rixnan mia matia,
mataki den apomene, ka8ws thn antikruzan,
    	xwris stalamatia.

Monaxa to tragoudi tous pws tairiaze olonwne
    	na skaei to mustiko:
-Xhra 8a geneis, 3ere to| ta nuxia mh se trwne
    	gi' arrevwniastiko.

Ki o diplanos t' aposwne: -Xare, ta roda koye
    	kai t' an8ia tou ntounia,
kai fer' ta mou kai strws' ta mou, sa 8a pe8anw apoye
    	s' authn th geitonia.

Kai to tragoudi gurize, varkoula apo th mpanta,
    	ston asiklh amane.
K' h karotsada kapote me ta violia. Kai panta
    	sta panta refene.

Ki an h8ele thn petuxan sthn porta ths mian wra
    	-pou taxei as ta trava-
h kalamata anasurth kai to roloi sta fora,
    	ki o koukos tous strava.

Mono mhn elees agarmph, pou na peirazei, le3h
    	kai pare3hgh8ei,
giati, gia ena filotimo kanenas otan mple3ei,
    	mporei na skotw8ei.

Ki autoi to paineuontane pws eitan sto ntahliki
    	me kotsi kai kardia.
To grafan kai sto lazo tous me t' ashmi maniki
    	giomata kai fardia:

"Ths fulakhs ta sidera einai gia tous leventes.
    	Ax! vax! kakourga gh."
K' h Aggelika traviotane, na mhn akouei kouventes
    	kai t' onoma ths vgei.

Apotraviotan k' epairne mazi ths ton aera
    	kai thn epi8umia,
ki apomene t' apofwno san apo mia flogera
    	s' aperanth erhmia.

Ki apomenan t' afterouga, sto dromo petaroudia,
    	kai mes ston korniaxto.
Sa na yuxorraghsane kovontan ta tragoudia
    	sto stoma t' anoixto.

Agaphth mou,

                    O hlios eproxwrousen taxus, ameiliktos, eporfurouto o orizwn, kai o idios apwlesas thn ektuflwtikhn lamyin tou epetrepe eis tas periergous Semelas n' ateniswsi pros auton.
                    Apo ta 8alassia loutra hkouonto arxurohxoi gelwtes kai diekrine kaneis thn xrushn kefalhn kai thn melanokomon tolmhras kolumvhtrias na provallh kai na proxwrh pros to meros ths nhsou Antigonhs, enw oi gelwtes apo tou paraphgmatos twn loutrwn ediplasiazonto. Hto 8rhskeutikh O8wmanikh eorth kai evlepe kaneis tous minaredes tou Stampoul, ws swmata metewra, kai to Peran fwtizomenon siga-siga, osw o hlios proshggizen eis thn dusin tou. Eporfurw8h o lofos ths Antigonhs, opis8en ths opoias ekruvh to leukon ths hmeras astron, eisdusan, ws tolmhra kolumvhtria, entos ths xrusokuanou Propontidos.
                    Auta ola, an kai den m' aresoun diolou, me dieskedasan arketa kai malista tosw aperrofh8hn prospa8ousa na diakrinw thn tolmhran kolumvhtrian h opoia epestreye twra kai e3ekourazeto e3aplwmenh epi ths epifaneias ths 8alasshs, enw oligoi vostruxoi ugroi diefeugon ek tou adiavroxou kalummatos ths kefalhs ths, wste otan thn anegnwrisa kai htoimas8hn me xara na yi8urisw "h Ouran..." hs8an8hn mian xeira epi tou wmou mou kai hkousa thn fwnhn tou e3adelfou mou, yi8urizousan:
    - Agaphth Eulalia, swsth poihtria!
                    Etarax8hn, ekokkinhsa kai egurisa authn thn foran me ekplh3in anupokriton, teinousa thn xeira mou pros ton e3adelfon mou, o opoios me evoh8hse na eger8w. Tote eidon kai ton 3enon, ton opoion di' eukolian wnomasa "xruswruxeion" kai eteina pros auton thn xeira mou, thn opoian edex8h eugnwmonws kai e8liyen elafrws.
    - Ma ti ekamnes olomonaxh s' auto to erhmo meros;
    - Ax, Alkiviadh, giati na me 3upnhshs apo to wraion oneiron, eis to opoion m' erriyen h fusis !
    - Hto tosw apogohteutikh h afupnhsis; eipe to "xruswruxeion" meta melagxolikhs pikrias.
    - Me sugxwreite, egw den gnwrizw thn glwssan twn saloniwn, eimai ligaki agria. Ptaiw an sas eipa mian alh8eian; Thn fusin, thn opoian onomazomen e3oxon, adikws thn agapw; Einai filh wraia, euais8htos, exemu8os, exei ola ta pronomia filhs. Di' auto den sunedesa filian me an8rwpinon plasma kai sunomilw me thn graian filhn mou, thn kurian Fusin, h opoia mou legei tosa pragmata.
    - Ti eutuxhs h fusis !
    - Dioti den apo8nhskei;
    - Einai polu mikron auto to proson| einai eutuxhs dioti agapatai.
    - Ths a3izei.
    - Apoye den 8a eis8e eis ton xoron;
    - Alh8eia, Eulalia, apoye 8a xash o xoros thn anegnwrismenhn vasilissan tou.
    - Den agapw ka8olou authn thn glwssan. An e3akolou8hs kat' auton ton tropon, adio den erxomai.
    - O 8eos uperhfanws antitassetai. Hmhn tosw uperhfanos pou 8a esthrizeto h reine du val eis ton vraxiona mou. Agaphth Eulalia, luphsou me.
                    Eixomen proxwrhsei eis ton elaiwna kai eida thn mama me mian filhn ths na trexoun pros anakaluyin mas anhsuxoi.
                    Exairethsa tous duo neous afou eipa:
    - Mh luphsai apo twra, pi8anon na el8w.
                    Esthrix8hn eis ton vraxiona ths mamas, h opoia me hrwta me anuponhsian.
    - Otan f8asoume sto 3enodoxeio, ola 8a sas ta pw xwris na 3exasw oute ena kai, ma twra uparxei kindunos na mas akousoun.
                    O xoros edideto eis to sxoleion ths Koinothtos kai o e3adelfos mou mas parekalese na riywme mia matia epi ths diakosmhsews.
                    Den eleipan ta persika xalia, ai shmaiai, ta an8h. Idiws to an8inon plaision, to opoion estefe thn eikona tou agaphtou mas Soultanou, hto kallitexnhma.
                    Eis mian gwnian ths ai8oushs, hsan ekte8eimena ta ergoxeira ta opoia ergazontai me toshn kalais8hsian ta mikra xerakia twn korasiwn kai ta opoia ekti8entai eis laxeion, to pro ion tou opoiou, enoumenon meta tou pro iontos tou xorou, einai h spoudaiotera ths sxolhs prosodos.
                    Efaga eis thn koinhn trapezan kai o kurios "xruswruxeion" tosw efrontize na me peripoihtai, wste elhsmonei na trwgh.
                    Enw epairname ton kafe, mou eipe:
    - Alh8eia, 8a el8ete sto xoro; Ti eutuxia! Mou didete to prwto vals; Eimai apaithtikos;
    - To prwto vals; dhl. to diko mou prwto. Dioti egw 8a el8w arga kai 8a meinw oligon. Den eimai polu kala. To vals to edwka tou e3adelfou mou.
    - wste mou menei h katrilia, na elpisw;
    - Nai.
                    3eureis ti dunami exw ston eauton mou. Amesws phra ena pothri koniak, aleiya to proswpon mou me lanolinhn kai epesa sthn klinhn mou, opou o upnos, o opoios 8a mou edide xrwmata wraia, den hrghse na m' episkef8h, ws na ton eixa paraggelia, h ws na ton dieta3en h megalof8almos Hra.
                    Ai trellai korai pou den kator8wnoun na koimh8oun, prin na upagoun sto xoro! Poson xanoun dioti den koimwntai kai den trwgoun apo thn sugkinhsin twn!
                    H mama omws hgrupnei h kahmenh, dia na m' e3upnhsh stas endeka.
                    E3upnhsa kai epluna to proswpon mou me xliaro nero kai eforesa oligh xlwmh poudra. Eprepe na me vlephs mesa eis to vleu ciel surah forema mou. 8a sou efainomhn 8eoths fantastikh h neraida ths Propontidos, opws o kurios "xruswruxeion" me wnomase. Ta mallia mou exrusizon polu, alla dia na xrusizoun perissoteron, eskorpisa pollh xrush poudra epanw twn. Ta an8h mou hsan drosera, wraia, kai h kamelia mou megaloprephs, opws h despoina twn. Mesa apo ta meta3ina gaza epefaineto ena trigwnon tou sth8ous mou, dia thn marmarinon tou opoiou leukothta e3wdeusa olo to koutaki ths poudras.
                    Mesa sth sala tou xorou hsan pollai wraiai, ma olai exasan apo ligaki, dioti allai ekouras8hsan, allwn ai endumasiai ezarwsan, kai dioti telos pantwn ta vlemmata sunh8isan na tas vlepoun epi tosas wras na gurizoun eis tou enos kai tou allou thn agkalhn.
                    Diekrina thn anian eis tous of8almous tou "xruswruxeiou" mou, all' ama me anegnwrisen upo thn nean kai megalopreph authn metamorfwsin mou, tosw wraian, tosw 8riamveutikhn, oi of8almoi tou aphstrayan kai ekarfw8hsan epanw mou me anupokriton en8ousiasmon.
                    Egw, ka8ws vevaia 8a to upo8eths, prospoih8hka pws den ton eida.
                    Hl8an oi kaluteroi neoi na eggrafoun eis ton katalogon twn sugxoreutwn mou, all' oloi euron thn authn tuxhn.
                    Tosw o kurios "xruswruxeion" emeine mageumenos na me vleph xoreuousan to prwton mou vals, me ton eutuxh e3adelfon, wste elhsmonhse na xoreush kai ekeinos, ote pros megalhn tou dusareskeian, o k. T. exwn adelfhn gia 3epoulhma kai nomisas oti to "xruswruxeion", ws 3enos, sustelletai na zhthsh sugxoreutrian, tou prosefere thn adelfhn tou, h opoia eixe mia wraia elia sto laimo ths, pou eyi8urizeto oti hto texnhth.
                    Egw ekama ena peripaton kai ezhthsa ena pagwto.
                    Trigurw mou esxhmatis8h eurutatos kuklos kai hrxise mia sundiale3is, ths opoias to kaiomenon livanwton apeu8uneto pros eme.
                    Hl8e kai to "xruswruxeion" me thn ntama tou kai exairetise melagxolikws. 
                    Otan metevhmen eis thn ai8ousan tou xorou kai h mousikh hrxise to proanakrousma, o lewn autos o asugkinhtos, hl8e deilos kai sunestalmenos, na mou upen8umish thn uposxesin mou.
                    8eleis perissotera; Eis ekeinon ton eutuxismenon tetraxoron eipame tosa polla wste... den mas emeinen allo apo ton papa kai ta stefania.
                    Den hto omws "xruswruxeion" o Nikolaos, hto dhl. alh8inon xruswruxeion aretwn kai kalwn ais8hmatwn, alla plousios den hto.
                    Eimai omws eutuxhs me ton Niko mou, m' agapa, ton agapw kai eime8a apo ta liga eutuxismena androguna.
                    Twra, auta sou ta egraya dia na prospa8hshs na wfelh8hs apo thn didaskalian twn, an omws sou fanoun mesa aniera kai tapeinwtika, ptaieis esu.
                    Nomizeis oti kai oi andres den paizoun tetoia paignidia;
A... autoi, ama krufodiale3oun kamian kurian "xruswruxeion" amesws, me spanion dia to fulon twn texnhn, paizoun temaxia kwmwdiwn kai dramatwn, me toshn teleiothta, tosa anekdota dihgountai monomaxiwn kai erwtikwn 8riamvwn, wste pollakis kataktwsin me toioutous akrovolismous to poliorkoumenon epiteleion, an den to fulattoun kerveroi, dhl. goneis kai loipoi, katafeugoun eis mesa viaia kai alh8ws aniera - ek twn opoiwn en einai eis hmas gnwston: h apagwgh.
                    wste vlepeis oti makarioi oi apatwntes! Afhse tas gerontikas ideas sou kai as se parasurh en sfodron reuma to opoion parasurei tosous kai tosous... Loipon... xa-xa-xa-xa!
                    Fantasou, h prospa8hson na fantas8hs tinos eirwnikon proswpaki anekaluya pisw apo ton wmo mou, na diavazh autas tas empisteutikas grammas... O Nikos diavase ola ta kator8wmata ths Lilhs tou| ekeinos twra ennoei na valh uposhmeiwseis kai na pros8esh 8aumastika, diamfisvhtounta thn au8entikothta ths dihghsews mou.                     Se glukofilw -oxi se glukofiloumen (etsi to 8elei o kurios Nikos).


                                                                          H Eulalia sou 

Ki o Erwtas, pou apeikaze ta krufoklahmata tous,
    	eskuve na tous pei,
pws to koritsi apofeuge na steketai konta tous,
    	na, etsi, apo ntroph.

Ma dixws allo lagiase ki akouei to ntavatouri,
    	ki ap' olous pio kala,
gia pisw apo t' agioklhma, gia pisw ap' to pantzouri,
    	gi' auto den to sfala.

Ftanei n' akouei ki as kleinetai ki as kruvetai opou 8elei.
    	To peisma pio gero.
"Aggelikoula zaxarh, ki Aggelikoula meli,
    	kai san to kruo nero."

"Aggelikoula zaxarh ki Aggelikoula meli"
    	-to 3analeei h seira-
"ki Aggelikoula kruo nero, pou pinoun oi Aggeloi."
    	Kai pali mia fora.

Me to vradaki tarxizan, to teleiwnan oi augoules.
    	(Ma esu kardia, ti ftais;)
Skazane kai plantazane gurw oi geitonopoules|
    	nies eitane ki autes.

Ma eitane mia h Aggelika. Ki o kosmos o dikos ths,
    	zwh, xara mazi.
An zei, as to ma8ei ot' eimouna k' egw agaphtikos ths.
    	Mporei kai na mh zei
